Important News

Central Party Headquarters and National Government Memorial Week

▲ At the Central Party Headquarters on the morning of the 11th, the Central Party Headquarters held the eighth weekly memorial service for the late Premier. Present were Central Committee members Ju Zheng, Chen Mingshu, Hong Luidong, Wang Qi, Zheng Zhanan, Li Zonghuang, Chu Minyi, Li Ciwen, Xiao Zhongzhen, Xiao Jishan, Xie Zuomin, Huang Fusheng, and staff Lai Bao, totaling more than 600 people. Ju Zheng presided over the meeting. After the salutations, Chen Mingshu reported, stating that many unfortunate events and changes in the political situation were caused by careless speech. This can be called a disease of the times. The central government has been established for more than ten days, but it has been silent and ineffective, failing to live up to the expectations of the people and comrades. Everyone can understand the content, environment, and responsibilities of the government by reading the speech of President Sun. Mr. Sun spoke very realistically, and the conclusion is to ask the leaders to unite. Without the leadership of the leaders, we are very empty, very scattered, and without strength to support this critical situation. The efforts of the brothers in the past few days have also been for this matter. I would like to briefly report on the past few days. Mr. Wang's illness is very troublesome. He had more than a dozen injections a week ago, and his diabetes decreased to about 110 degrees. Later, some comrades from Beijing came to Shanghai, and after talking for two or three hours in front of his sickbed, he fainted and his diabetes increased to 140 degrees. Therefore, he needs to be re-diagnosed and rested quietly. Mr. Wang is eager to come to Beijing. Although he is ill, it can be said that his heart has already arrived in Beijing. Regarding Mr. Hu, Shu had sent two or three telegrams and the members from Guangdong had also sent telegrams urging him to come to Beijing. Comrades Liu Ziyin and Wu Tiayun went to Hong Kong, and recently the Central Committee also sent Comrade Yu Youren to persuade him. Regarding Mr. Jiang, Shu also sent four telegrams urging him to return to Beijing. Many comrades have visited him one after another, but no reply has been received. The current diplomatic situation is serious, and it is a matter of national survival, relying entirely on the leadership of the leaders. Comrades Sun Zhesheng, Wu Tiecheng, Kong Yongzhi, and Li Junpei went to Fenghua today to urge Mr. Jiang to come forward. The center of a country is related to safety and danger, and the center should be established as soon as possible so that the party and government can be promoted. It is expected that the three leaders will return soon. Now that a great enemy is at hand, we must fight desperately, and all interests, rights, wrongs, and emotions are unnecessary. The unfortunate conflicts between comrades in the past should be resolved and we should embrace each other and cry. We also hope that all comrades will come to the central government and stand on the front line to save the people from disaster in order to solve the current problems. Looking at the current situation, it seems to have become a retreat from the revolution, gradually reaching the end of the road. If the center of the revolution cannot be united and allowed to sink, it will end silently. We must reverse the retreat and re-arouse it, otherwise there is no way to help. In case the three leaders do not come, or are late in coming, and the center is not established and the government is not stable, we cannot wait to die. No matter what, we must support ourselves and fight forward, fighting for the personality of the party and the country, and fighting for the life of the nation, regardless of success or failure, profit or loss, life or death. If we cannot revive the revolutionary spirit of the fourteenth and fifteenth years of the Republic of China, this retreat will not be reversed. Disaster is imminent, and we cannot wait. Everyone must cheer up and seek our way out. The meeting adjourned after the report.

▲ On the same morning, the National Government held the weekly memorial service for the late Premier. Present were Chairman Lin Sen, and ministers and officials of various departments Chen Mingshu, Zhu Peide, Ru Yuli, Chen Shaokuan, Wei Huai, Lu Chao, and others, as well as staff and guests, totaling more than 200 people. Chairman Lin Sen presided over the meeting, led the salutations, and then gave a speech [Wholeheartedness and Consistency from Beginning to End], the original words are as follows: [Today is Memorial Week, and we will talk about the Premier's teachings. Now, let's take the two sentences from the party song that was just sung, "Wholeheartedness and Consistency from Beginning to End," and read them. This party song was originally a school motto made by the Premier for the Whampoa Military Academy and used as a guideline for training armed comrades. The armed comrades who studied at that time were able to abide by this school motto and remain committed to it, so they later made many contributions to the party and the country when they went on the Northern Expedition. After the Northern Expedition was completed and the country was unified, the reason for this was that the comrades generally worked hard to follow this school motto. Today, I am bringing up these two sentences to talk about so that everyone can deeply understand the meaning of these eight characters. So-called "Wholeheartedness," is to ask everyone to concentrate on what they do, and at the same time, in addition to concentration, they must also have a persistent spirit, so after the sentence "Wholeheartedness," there is the sentence "Consistency from Beginning to End." Only by being able to be consistent from beginning to end can things be done successfully. We often hear a very common saying in society, that is, "Nothing is difficult in the world, but only fear of not being focused." It can be seen that difficult things are not to be feared, but lack of focus is what is to be feared. The Premier saw this, so he taught the comrades that whatever they do for the party and the country, they should do it with concentration and perseverance, and at the same time, they must continue to work hard to be consistent from beginning to end, so that there is hope of completion and hope of victory. According to what our sages said, there is also a saying, "A man without constancy cannot be a witch or a doctor." The ancients meant to regard witch doctors as small things that cannot be done because everything, whether big or small, has its difficulties. If you do not have perseverance and encounter difficulties, you will stop or abandon it, and you will inevitably become halfway, and naturally you will not be able to achieve the hope of success. Today, taking advantage of the opportunity of Memorial Week, I would like to specially bring up these eight characters and talk to you about them, hoping that everyone will often reflect on themselves, put them into practice, and make these two great teachings of the Premier show great achievements under the concerted efforts of all comrades.]

The Truth About the Withdrawal of Defense from Jinzhou

The withdrawal of defense from Jinzhou is of great importance. The reporter has personally visited Qinhuangdao, Shanhaiguan, and other places, observed with a cold eye, and explored in many ways. The information obtained is somewhat different from the outside reports and the records in various newspapers. A summary is recorded below:

The reporter arrived in Tianjin on the 29th. Tianjin newspapers mostly reported how fierce the fighting was on the front line, while on the other hand, there were rumors that the main force of the Northeast Army was already withdrawing. On the morning of the 30th, I rushed to the front. On the way through Tanggu, there were Japanese soldiers conducting exercises in the same car. The Japanese army in Tianjin has reached 3,000 people, and they are constantly carrying out exercises, the purpose of which is to prevent the deployment of our army's war equipment. Since the beginning of winter, the sea traffic between Dalian and Tianjin has used Tanggu as its port. The Japanese reinforcements to Tianjin must be transported by train from Tanggu. Therefore, Japanese soldiers travel back and forth between Tianjin and Tanggu in an endless stream. The Japanese army, as usual, only pays half the fare for the train and keeps an account, not paying in cash. It is said that the Japanese army owes the Beining Railway more than one million yuan in freight charges. When the train stopped at Qinhuangdao, I saw a building at the station with about four rooms full of Japanese soldiers. A Japanese soldier stood in front of the door, acting as a guard. Three Japanese soldiers stood inside the door. One held a telephone and constantly spoke, presumably reporting the train traffic situation to his superiors. Four Japanese warships were berthed at Qinhuangdao. One of them then sailed to Shanhaiguan. Shanhaiguan originally had three Japanese gunboats and one aircraft carrier berthed there. On the 31st, another gunboat was added, which came from Qinhuangdao. Shanhaiguan originally had about 100 Japanese garrison troops stationed there due to the Boxer Protocol, but this has recently been increased to more than 200 people. The area where the team is stationed has complete fortifications such as barbed wire and trenches, and it is said that tunnels were dug long ago, but it is not known where they now lead. Shanhaiguan also has Italian and French troops stationed there, but the number is not large.

Shanhaiguan is defended by the Independent 9th Brigade, whose commander is He Zhuguo. He is from Guangxi and graduated from the Japanese Military Academy. The reporter once sent a card to visit him and was received. He is very knowledgeable about the history of Japanese aggression in the Northeast and important issues in the Northeast, such as railway commercial lease rights. When asked about military plans, he sighed loudly, saying that the duty of soldiers is to defend the territory and the country. If the Japanese army invades, he will resist to the death, but if Jinzhou is not defended, Shanhaiguan will be in danger with the enemy, and he will really not be able to do anything. When necessary, he will only have to die to repay the country.

Shanhaiguan is only a few miles from the coast. The Japanese warships' artillery fire can reach the area directly with plenty to spare. There are no mountains along the coast, and there is no way to defend against the navy. Moreover, the Japanese side originally had garrison troops stationed there, and the aircraft carrier is berthed here, using the sea, land, and air forces together. With a small number of troops (He's brigade has a total of 10,000 people, but they are stationed in Lutai, Yuguan, and various places along the Beining Railway), how can he resist? Therefore, Yuguan has long been lost to us. Now there is no great significance in defending or not defending. It is truly difficult for He's brigade.

Shanhaiguan has always been the gateway to the Northeast, and the people of the country all know its importance. However, with the mountains extending outwards, it is very difficult to enter the pass. Now, the Japanese army has occupied the danger to the west from the east. Shanhaiguan has no danger to defend, and not only does Shanhaiguan have no danger to defend, but also all places west of Shanhaiguan are the same. The Beining Railway runs along the coast, and it is protected by towering mountains. Everywhere is under the threat of Japanese warships' artillery fire. How can we survive? Therefore, if Jinzhou is not defended, Tianjin will be in the hands of the Japanese. The construction of the Beining Road never considered national defense plans in those years. In addition, the Boxer Protocol allowed the demolition of the Dagu Forts and allowed foreigners to station troops and transport troops along the line. Alas, can this be called an independent country? The military authorities of our country are only busy with internal wars and neglect national defense, and it has come to this. To the east of Shanhaiguan, the lands of Suizhong, Xingcheng, and Jinzhou are surrounded by mountains, which are not within the reach of the Japanese navy, and it is not difficult to defend them. The reporter once met with officials of the temporary provincial government of Jinzhou. According to them, the trenches in Jinzhou were completed long ago, and the war materials prepared were also quite sufficient. If defended tightly, they can be supported for at least two months. According to the troops stationed in the Jinzhou area, in addition to the 12th, 19th, and 20th Brigades, there are also the gendarmerie cavalry brigade, training team, plainclothes team, etc., totaling no less than 50,000 people. Even if Goubangzi is lost and Dahu Mountain is not guaranteed, if they retreat to Jinzhou, they can fight hand-to-hand for a while. If Jinzhou also falls, Xingcheng and Suizhong have dangers to defend. Moreover, volunteer armies have already risen up in the interior of eastern provinces, which can greatly disturb the rear of the Japanese army. Even if the Japanese army is all-powerful, they will definitely not be able to eliminate our army within two or three months and reach Yuguan and link up with their navy. Moreover, when the Japanese army launched the invasion of Jinzhou, the United Kingdom, the United States, and France had warned Japan. If it lasts for a long time, the international situation will definitely change. How can the Japanese army be sure of winning? Now, everything east of Yuguan is under the occupation of the Japanese army, and there is no danger to defend west of Yuguan. It is like a Japanese defense zone. There are still people in the country who are demanding that the government recover the lost territory by force. I don't know how they will enter the eastern provinces, or how to transport troops and military equipment.

According to various news agencies, it seems that when the Japanese army attacked Jinzhou, our army fought fiercely with them, but eventually withdrew due to lack of strength. But according to what I have heard, those who fought against the Japanese army were volunteer armies composed of students, veterans, and [bandits] of the Republic of China. As for the official army of the Northeast, they did not fire a single shot at the Japanese army, but withdrew automatically. When the Japanese army launched the attack on Jinzhou, reports said that Rong Zhen returned to Ping from Jin, saying nothing, and then went to Xiehe Hospital for medical treatment. At that time, Zhang Xueliang was negotiating with Japan, and the Japanese side agreed to go as far as Da Linghe (a station east of Jinzhou). The Northeast army withdrew to within the customs, and the Jinzhou provincial government allowed it to exist, which is the so-called neutral zone realized in an invisible way. Rong Zhen then returned to Jin and ordered all the troops to withdraw to within the customs. The 12th Brigade, stationed between Changli County, first withdrew on the 29th, followed by the 20th Brigade and the 19th Brigade. All brigades withdrew to within the customs on the 31st. Rong Zhen's special train arrived in Luan County on the afternoon of the 1st. When the withdrawal began, the main force of the Japanese army was still in Xinmin, but they soon tracked them down, bypassed Jinzhou, and headed for Shanhaiguan. The aircraft carrier berthed in the Bohai Sea (near Shanhaiguan) sent out planes to force Shanhaiguan and welcome the advance of the Japanese army. All personnel of the Northeast Frontier Defense Army Headquarters in Jinzhou left Jinzhou on the 31st, and the temporary provincial government also disappeared invisibly. The Northeast authorities have always adhered to a policy of non-resistance. I don't know where their intentions lie. (Published in Tianjin on January 7)

The Problem of Traffic on the Beining Railway

Tianjin correspondence: The Beining Railway, since the Japanese army's invasion on September 18th, has been repeatedly devastated by the Japanese army in various sections outside the pass. The railway property has been destroyed, the employees have been injured and killed, and the losses of public and private property are incalculable. However, the internal and external employees still hold the spirit of perseverance, defying all dangers and overcoming all difficulties, and do their best to maintain traffic. The national and provincial institutions outside the pass have been swept away by the Japanese army. The only thing that the people of the Northeast rely on to communicate with the interior is the Beining Railway. Since the incident, the passenger train on the section outside the pass has never been stopped for more than a day, so the news is relatively well-informed, and its contribution to traffic is also very great. However, since the withdrawal of our army from Jinzhou, all employees on the trunk road outside the pass have lost their protection. Feeling the coercion of the Japanese army, they have to temporarily avoid it, so they made an orderly withdrawal, while retaining a small number of important staff stationed in the major stations. However, due to the Japanese military operations, the four passenger trains that left ahead of schedule were unable to return. Later, as our army had all withdrawn into the customs and the Japanese army had advanced to Wanjiatun, the first station outside Shanhaiguan, it gradually became peaceful in recent days. The Railway Bureau is eager to seek to resume traffic, so it sent Hu Chunzan, the former director of the Shenyang Office, and the original employees of each section and station, to go east from Shanhaiguan on January 5th. When they arrived in Xingcheng, they met the commander of the Japanese army stationed there and negotiated the traffic method. The commander said that he was only responsible for military affairs, and the matter of traffic had to be discussed with the current Fengtian Transportation Committee. (According to Shenyang originally set up the Northeast Transportation Committee, which was moved to Beiping after September 18th. The current Transportation Committee is an organization composed of committees appointed under the control of the Japanese. The chairman of the committee is Ding Jianxiu.) Mr. Hu reported this result to the Tianjin General Bureau. At the same time, the General Bureau also received a telegram from Shenyang from the Director of Transport and Jian of the road, an Englishman, saying that there was no problem with the traffic of the entire road, but according to the Japanese consul stationed in Shenyang, it must be discussed with the new government here before it can be implemented. After receiving these two reports, the Railway Bureau believes that since there is a traitorous pseudo-Transportation Committee in the middle, it is feared that the traffic on the entire road will not be easy to achieve in the near future. Since the road has a Sino-British company loan relationship, the representative of the Sino-British company stationed on the road, that is, the current English manager of the road's accounting office, in cooperation with the English chief of the engineering department, went to Ping from Tianjin on January 8 to meet with the British Minister, and to discuss the solution to the traffic problem, or to ask the government to examine it. According to recent reliable sources, the pseudo-Transportation Committee under the control of the current Japanese wants to imitate the previous example and rename the section outside the customs as the Shanfeng Road (that is, from Shanhaiguan to Fengtian) to be managed by the association. The position of director has been assigned to Kan Duo. Kan was the director of the Jiaoji Railway Bureau. If this saying becomes a reality, the problem of traffic on the Beining Road will be more difficult to solve. (January 9)

Zhang Jinghui Publicly Takes Office as Chairman of Heilongjiang

▲ Issued a Circular Telegram Stating That He Was Urged by the People of Heilongjiang

▲ All Organizations Imitate the Liaoning and Jilin Methods

▲ The Special Zone Garrison Team Will Be Expanded into a Brigade

Harbin correspondence: There are two things that happened here around the time of the New Year, which, because of strict security, have only now been learned. The records are as follows: ▲The Garrison Team's Mutiny Failed to Materialize The junior officers of the special zone garrison team newly recruited by Zhang Jinghui are mostly graduates of the new special zone police academy. Young and hot-blooded, their love of country is no less than others. However, since the team was established, the Harbin people have scolded it as a traitorous team. Anyone who passes by the team's station must tell each other, which the officers and soldiers heard and felt quite embarrassed. Guan Lu, the third company commander of the first battalion, and Wang Yue, the first company commander of the second battalion, thought of making achievements to get out of the situation. They secretly contacted the platoon leaders, intending to unite the officers and soldiers of the first and second battalions to raise the banner of the National Salvation Army and go to Hailun to join Ma Zhanshan. After a long period of brewing, by the end of last month, all officers and soldiers had been contacted and agreed. They also planned to coerce Lin Yuzhao, the director of education of the police academy, to be the leader in order to appeal. Three days before New Year's Eve, Lin was taken from his private residence. They planned to launch the mutiny late at night on New Year's Eve, first coercing the fourth battalion and the special battalion to act in unison, shelling the Japanese Consulate on Jilin Street in Nangang, and then using infantry to drive and kill the Japanese residents on Daoli and Daowai streets. Then they would break into the Qiulin department store, a large White Russian merchant, and each person would take a woolen blanket. They would then seize all the cars in the city, set off firecrackers, and parade through the streets for a week before heading to Hulan north of the river to gather and then go to see Ma Gushan to surrender. However, the day before the uprising, Lin Yuzhao suddenly claimed that his qualifications were far inferior to those of the chief captain Yu Bianwan, and he was willing to accompany two or three people to persuade Yu to be the leader. The platoon leaders did not notice and accompanied Lin to Yu's residence. Lin immediately told Yu the mutiny plan of the two teams. Yu immediately detained the few people who went, and then went to the first and second battalion stations overnight to convene the police officers for a speech, using the friendship of teachers and students (Yu was the director of education of the police academy). The platoon leaders, seeing that the opportunity had been revealed, agreed to stop the matter. Guan Lu and Wang Yue, who advocated the mutiny, were also replaced, and the matter ended. Now, most of the police officers in each team have been replaced to prevent another incident. According to reports, the entire temporary garrison team has more than 2,300 people. Except for the third battalion, which was sent to Heihe, about 1,800 people are in Harbin. Zhang Jinghui still feels that the troops are weak, and he has recently agreed with the Japanese to add five battalions, each with 500 people, divided into four companies, one company under the jurisdiction of three platoons, and attached special teams such as mortars, flat-fire guns, and machine guns. The plan is being prepared, and the guns have arrived in Heihe from Tao'ang Road due to the Eastern Railway's refusal to transport them. It will be established at the latest next month. It is said that after the newly added troops are formed, they will be organized into a brigade together with the previously recruited troops. It is said that Yu Jingtao, the current chief captain, will be the brigade commander.

▲ Zhang Jinghui's Circular Telegram on Taking Office Zhang Jinghui issued a circular telegram on the night of the 1st. The telegram was sent in code, and few people outside knew about it. The original text is said to be as follows: [Since the September 18th Incident in Heilongjiang, Chairman Ma Zhanshan has moved to Hailun, and no one is in charge of provincial administration. The people are panicked and public security is worrying. The representatives of Heilongjiang have repeatedly urged Jinghui to go to Harbin to preside over and temporarily maintain the status quo. Their words are sincere and urgent, and I cannot refuse. In addition to sending Deputy Police Chief Ying Shun to temporarily maintain public security in the provincial capital, I will formally take office as the Chairman of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government on the 1st of this month. All organizations will imitate the Provincial Governor's Office of Fengtian and the Chief Executive's Office of Jilin. Everything does not seek change, as long as the status quo is maintained. Jinghui, with his mediocre talents, has been entrusted with this important task, especially in this time of national and local turmoil. I am even more afraid of failing to live up to expectations. I hope that my fellow colleagues will give me corrections from time to time.] The telegram did not list titles at the end, only signed Zhang Jinghui. Around 12 o'clock that night, someone was sent to the telegraph office and ordered to send it urgently. Unexpectedly, at 1:00 a.m. on the 2nd, he suddenly ordered someone to take it back, saying that it would not be sent. Then, after 2:00 a.m., he sent the order to send it immediately. In addition to sending it to Xi Qia of Jilin and Jian Shi Yi of Liaoning, it was only sent to the various agencies in Harbin. It was not sent to the interior or to Ma Zhanshan's office. It is said that a few days ago, Japanese Army Commander Honjo Shigeru and Chief of Staff Itagaki came to Harbin to force Zhang to express his attitude. Zhang was forced to issue this telegram. At the same time, Ying Shun, Zhang's representative in Heilongjiang, was ordered to carry out the organization of the provincial government, first restoring the three departments of civil affairs, finance, and propaganda. Zhang may go to Heihe within a few days to hold an inauguration ceremony. (January 4)

White Russian Disturbances Continue

▲ Repeated Attacks on Police Stations

▲ Japanese Covertly Instigating

Harbin Dispatch: Following the White Russian rioters' incident, police in full uniform patrolled Central Avenue from 9 p.m. on the 4th, prohibiting pedestrians from entering each intersection. Around 10 p.m., all Russians except Chinese were barred from passing. At 10:30 p.m., over ten Russian rioters fired a volley at the Daoli Yangcaoshi police station, prompting the station to extinguish its lights and scatter them. At 11 p.m., the rioters moved to the First Precinct, firing at the Shaman Street police station and shattering its door lamp. The station responded with gunfire, and the rioters proceeded to the First Precinct's entrance, intending to shoot inside. The guard on duty noticed this and fired a volley, scattering the rioters. At 11:10 p.m., the Xidaqiao outpost of the Nangang Third Precinct was also besieged by over forty Russian rioters. The outpost returned fire, and after a ten-minute standoff, the rioters were driven back. One rioter was captured on the scene, found to possess a war knife and an Imperial Russian military flag. When questioned about his name, he remained silent. Security was tightened last night, with over a thousand members of the Provisional Garrison's First Battalion deployed. The situation gradually eased today, but it is anticipated that the rioters will launch planned attacks tonight. Officials have confirmed that the Japanese consulate is instigating this, paying each rioter twenty-five yuan in gold notes redeemable upon presentation. The Japanese consulate's scheme aims to: first, have the consular body claim that the Harbin authorities are unable to maintain order, necessitating international co-management and the deployment of Japanese troops to Harbin; second, target Wang Duanhua, the chief of the Special Police, specifically because he is associated with Zhang Xueliang and considered by the Japanese to be connected to the old Northeast regime, creating panic to protest to Zhang Jinghui and remove him from his position. The Russian-language newspaper run by the Japanese has been exaggerating news about police shootings in the past two days, claiming that several innocent White Russians were injured, with the intention of inciting animosity and pushing White Russians toward extremism. On the evening of the 4th, the Governor's Office held a special meeting regarding this matter, attended by Zhang Jinghui, Wang Ruihua, Ding Chao, and Xing Zhanqing, among others. Someone reported the Japanese conspiracy to Zhang, who became very angry and slammed the table, saying, "I have already accommodated the Japanese in everything, hoping that the region would not be ruined, only to earn the reputation of a traitor. What more dissatisfaction do the Japanese have? They must create a chaotic situation. If that's the case, then we must officially take action. Even if I sacrifice my old life, I will not regret it." Ding Chao was also quite angry, saying, "Since the White Russians are so unappreciative, fortunately, we still have two brigades of troops here. We might as well fight them." Subsequently, those who advocated for reconciliation advised Zhang to visit the Japanese consulate to inquire about the Japanese's true intentions and express our determination to maintain order. Zhang immediately went to the Japanese consulate that night, visited Oashi Chūichi, and had a lengthy discussion. The Japanese consul firmly denied instigating the White Russian riots, only promising to suppress the Russian-language newspaper to prevent the situation from escalating due to propaganda. After Zhang returned to his office, he informed the leaders, saying, "Let's wait and see for a day or two." On the night before last (the 3rd), when the Russian rioters attacked Xiaowen Street, they threw a hand grenade at the police. The rioters fled to Xin'anbu that night, where five were intercepted by the Fifth Special Police Precinct. They found a pistol, stolen from a precinct police officer. The names of these five are: Marcheinko Vitte, 19 years old; Nikowei Yevich, 31 years old; Magosiknow, 18 years old; Mage Bowaite, 27 years old. After being sent to the Investigation Bureau, they have not confessed. However, it was discovered that these five Russians had previously been imprisoned several times for theft and had just been released. On the police side, two have died, both garrison soldiers: Liu Jingrui and Sheng Fuduo. (January 5th)

Continued Report on the Assassination Case in Fuzhou

▲ The Provincial Government Completely Bans Anti-Japanese Movements

▲ And Provides a Solatium of 50,000 Yuan to the Deceased

▲ But Public Sentiment is Agitated and the Market Remains Tense

Fuzhou Dispatch: Regarding the assassination of the Japanese elementary school teacher Mito Sanuo and his wife in Fuzhou, although the provincial government has offered a reward of 10,000 yuan to capture the murderers, four days have passed without a breakthrough. According to observations from various sources, it is believed that the murderers were Japanese or Taiwanese, and the case is significantly related to romantic issues, having nothing to do with our side. However, three Japanese warships, including the "Ayashi," entered Mawei around 8 a.m. on the 7th, leading to widespread rumors that Japanese sailors would land and be stationed in the Cangqianshan and Fan Chuanpu areas on the south bank of the Taijiang River. Rumors spread, and public sentiment became agitated. Rice and foreign currency prices suddenly soared. Exchanging paper money for foreign currency required a premium of ten cents per yuan, and the price of white rice also jumped from 11.5 yuan to 12 yuan per shi (unit of measure). Therefore, on the afternoon of the 7th, the provincial government issued a proclamation, stating, in brief, that the government would take responsibility for handling recent diplomatic incidents, but rumors were rampant. During this period of martial law, spreading rumors was inexcusable. In addition to ordering military and police organs to strictly investigate and handle the matter, the proclamation was issued to inform all merchants and residents to live and work in peace, not to heed rumors lightly, and to avoid causing disturbances. This was of utmost importance. After the proclamation was issued, the market atmosphere remained tense because the military and police had not yet lifted martial law.

Page 10

Furthermore, on the afternoon of the 7th, Lin Zhiyuan, a member of the provincial government, toured the city and public places with the Japanese consul. The Japanese consul expressed satisfaction upon seeing that anti-Japanese slogans and publications had been completely covered with other advertisements, and that various anti-Japanese groups had also disbanded in compliance with orders. As the Mito Sanuo couple's murder case was unrelated to our side, the provincial authorities would provide a solatium of 50,000 yuan to resolve the matter. The Japanese consul had agreed to halt the landing of sailors, and the warships might leave within a few days. (January 8th)

Han Fuju Takes Over National Tax Agencies

Jinan Dispatch: Han Fuju previously, due to the central government's arrears in paying the Third Route Army's salaries for several months, resulting in the inability of soldiers and officers to maintain their livelihoods, once ordered the takeover of Shandong's national tax agencies, such as the Salt Transportation Office, the Tobacco and Alcohol Stamp Tax Bureau, the Consolidated Tax Office, the Saltpeter Bureau, and the Lu Da Mining Tax Office, using central tax revenues to pay military expenses. Subsequently, Jiang Bocheng returned to Jinan from Beijing, indicating that the Third Route Army's expenses would still be the responsibility of Finance Minister Song Ziwen, who would be in charge of planning and allocating funds. Thereupon, Han again ordered the reversal of this decision, instructing all agencies to revert to their original status. Now, with Song's departure and the reorganization of the National Government, the Third Route Army's salaries are still not being allocated. Recently, the heads of national tax agencies in Shandong have become increasingly irresponsible. For example, Yuan Timing of the Salt Transportation Office has been in Beijing for over a month, and Xiang Jieren, the head of the Tobacco and Alcohol Stamp Tax Bureau, has also been traveling between Beijing and Jinan, effectively neglecting their duties. If this continues, tax revenues will be greatly affected. Today (the 9th), he specifically ordered Li Wuchen, the chief of the General Headquarters' Military Law Department, to serve as the Salt Transportation Commissioner, and Meng Zhaokong, the director of the Military Supplies Department, to serve as the head of the Tobacco and Alcohol Stamp Tax Bureau, taking over the two agencies again to facilitate reorganization. (Note: Li and Meng are the same individuals previously appointed to take over the Salt Transportation Office and the Tobacco and Alcohol Stamp Tax Bureau.) There is no news yet regarding the takeover of other national tax agencies. (January 9th)

Japanese Provoke Again in Wuhu

▲ Assaulting Boatmen, Sailors Landing

▲ Making Unreasonable Demands to the County Government

Wuhu Dispatch: Since news of Jinzhou's fall, the people of Wuhu have been heartbroken and doubly concerned about national salvation efforts. In addition to telegraphing the central government to declare its policy towards Japan, the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association yesterday sent a letter to the Wuhu Iron Blood Corps for National Salvation, urging them to go north immediately to kill the enemy and save the nation. A farewell meeting will be convened within days to boost morale, and a large banner has been specially made to be presented to the corps upon their departure, to embolden them. Chen Tiaoyuan, the chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government, has also telegraphed the National Government, requesting a swift determination of diplomatic strategy and expressing his willingness to lead the troops in Anhui and serve as a vanguard. However, the Japanese residents in Wuhu, seeing the progress of their country's aggression, are extremely arrogant and have been provoking us for days. Fortunately, our people have remained calm and patient and have not engaged with them. Unexpectedly, around 2 p.m. on the 9th, a Japanese man named Lin Zhengji changed into Chinese clothing, purchased a large amount of food, and hired a boat to transport it to the Japanese warship "Hirado" stationed in Wuhu. When the boatman, Sun Youcai, asked why he was impersonating a Chinese, the Japanese, being of a violent nature, suddenly struck Sun's head with an oar. The people on the river were outraged, but seeing that Sun's injuries were not life-threatening, they restrained themselves. Unexpectedly, the cunning Japanese, after boarding the "Hirado," fabricated a story and reported it to the ship's captain, who dispatched a large number of armed sailors to escort him ashore. He also fabricated a report to the Japanese Consul Shirasaki Hakuo. Without investigating the facts, the consul made unreasonable protests to the Wuhu County Government, demanding three points: 1) Strictly punish Sun Youcai; 2) Suppress the anti-Japanese movement; 3) Protect Japanese residents along the river. After receiving the protest, County Magistrate Yu Bohua not only refuted each point but also planned to lodge a serious protest, requesting the Japanese side to punish the culprit and apologize. It is unknown how this will be resolved. (9th)

Trend Towards Resolution of Fengxian Incident

Xuzhou Dispatch: Regarding the mutiny of the Third Cavalry Division stationed in Fengxian, Yu Huaizhong from the Jiangsu Provincial Party Headquarters, Han Shouqian from the Provincial Government, and Zhang Ruitang from the Pacification Commissioner's Office have successively arrived in Fengxian to investigate. The commissioners have now clarified the incident. It is said to have originated from the instigation and provocation of the grain department personnel. Most of the personnel in the grain department engaged in personal gain and corruption. Although County Magistrate Yang Liangyi dismissed them, the grain irregularities have not been completely resolved. The dismissed personnel, upon hearing the news that the Party Committee Dong YuJue and others were organizing a committee to investigate the accumulated malpractices of the grain department, feared that the accumulated malpractices would be exposed and the dismissed personnel would be held accountable. At a time when the local authorities were unable to cope with the Third Cavalry Division's supplies, the grain department personnel fabricated rumors that Dong YuJue and others were obstructing the supply, inciting military unrest, and colluding with the police force to take certain actions. The Third Cavalry Division had already been dissatisfied because the local authorities were unwilling to bear the burden of supplies. Consequently, some officers and soldiers were misled by them, and Zhang Zhankui did not investigate, resulting in a sudden disturbance, the capture and detention of Dong YuJue and others, and the removal of public funds and confiscation of firearms. Furthermore, the grain department personnel colluded with the soldiers of the division to burn all the grain records, in an attempt to destroy evidence. Thus, a serious situation was formed. People from all walks of life in Fengxian fled the area, accusing Commander Zhang of mutiny. Zhang, in turn, submitted a report to the Pacification Commissioner's Office, accusing Dong of being reactionary. In reality, Zhang was deceived by the schemes of others, and Dong and others were also unjustly tormented. After the commissioners completed their investigation, the gentry of Fengxian came forward to mediate, agreeing to two things: 1) All organs of Fengxian would send a telegram to restore the reputation of Commander Zhang, and bear the supplies designated by the Provincial Government; 2) Commander Zhang would release the detained personnel and return the confiscated firearms. With the mediation plan established, the commissioners left Fengxian separately to report back. Yesterday (the 9th), Yu Huaizhong, a member of the Provincial Party Headquarters, passed through Xuzhou southward. According to discussions, after the mediation of the gentry, the Fengxian incident may be resolved. (10th)

Local Communications

Songjiang

The Finance Bureau Strictly Urges the Conversion of Land Tax into Rice Tax: The land along the coast of this county is barren. Following the order of the provincial authorities to start collecting converted land tax into rice tax last year, the residents of the 15th district repeatedly requested a delay. The accumulated cases were substantial. After hearing that Jinshan and Fengxian, neighboring counties that had also been ordered to start collection, had been granted a delay, the residents of this district argued even more fiercely and even submitted a resolution for exemption at the fourth county administrative meeting. The county government, based on this, forwarded the request to the Finance Department. The order was received to still investigate and handle the matter according to the original plan and strictly urge the bureau to expedite the collection, without allowing any delays. After the Finance Bureau relayed this, it stated that the income from the conversion of land tax into rice tax had already been included in the budget, and any shortage would affect the designated expenditures. The order from the provincial authorities to expedite the transfer was urgent, so the bureau repeatedly persuaded the landowners to understand the situation and actively contribute, ensuring that the tax for this year and the past two years (years 18 and 19 of the Republic) was quickly paid into the treasury. If there were any further delays, the police would be ordered to arrest and escort them. If any local bullies were found obstructing, they would be severely punished. This notice was to inform all landowners.

The County Court President Transferred: Huang Liang, the president of the County Court, was transferred by order of the High Court to be promoted to judge of the High Court. Chen Ruizhen was appointed to succeed him as president. President Huang has now completed the handover and will go to Suzhou to assume his new position after the new president arrives in Songjiang today for the handover.

Robbery and Arson by Bandits: Chen Qixiu's house in Tiandu Ham, the 15th map of the southern suburbs, was robbed and set on fire. Around 1 a.m. on the 10th, while they were sound asleep, five or six bandits suddenly entered through a window in the small north-facing house. The family members heard the sound of footsteps but dared not investigate. They were robbed of one shi (unit of measure) of unpolished rice and other clothing items before the bandits left through the main gate. Before leaving, they set fire to the north-facing house and the south-facing厢房 (xiāngfáng, side room of a traditional Chinese house) in the courtyard. Straw was also placed at the entrance of the south-facing 厢房 in preparation for spreading the fire. Fortunately, people were immediately called to put out the fire, preventing a disaster.

Fengxian

A Detective Stationed in Shanghai Returned to His Native Place for Trial: Xu Rongxiang, a detective stationed in Shanghai by the County Public Security Bureau, was previously reported by Xi Lanqing, a detective stationed in Shanghai by the First District of the Water Police, for previously introducing Quan Wenjun and Zhao Guomin, former pseudo-regiment leaders under Taibao A Shu, to Xu Yabo, who had been sentenced by the Songjiang Court for the Xijing robbery, as his disciples. On suspicion of colluding with bandits, he was detained and sent to the province by the district in conjunction with the police last June. After questioning by the Zhenjiang Provincial Security Office, he denied any involvement. At the same time, the Supervisory Office of the County Public Security Bureau also investigated the officer's daily activities as ordered and provided a guarantee. Therefore, the office specially dispatched police yesterday (the 10th) to escort the detective back, ordering him to be handed over to the County Government for trial and verification.

Changshu

The Huitong Jinjiang Ferry Causes an Accident: Since the resumption of the Huitong regular ferry service between Suzhou and Changshu, business has been quite good. On the 9th, the bureau's Jinjiang small ferry, which departed from Changshu for Suzhou at 10 a.m., passed the Wuta area in the Yuanhe district. Cheng Yong, a villager from Hubin township, happened to be sailing a small boat nearby when it was struck by the Jinjiang ferry, causing the small boat to capsize immediately. All six people in the boat fell into the river. Fortunately, the ferry stopped immediately and tried to rescue them, preventing a major disaster. After negotiations, the Huitong Company compensated the small boat with 25 silver dollars for repairs, resolving the matter.

The Water Police Team Captures Two Bandits: Yang Qingjiu, the captain of the 13th Water Police Team stationed in Changshu, was ordered by the Suzhou District Department the other day to patrol the southern countryside. On the 10th, while patrolling the Yangshuyuan and Huananzhen areas in the Wang Yuanhe district, he learned that several suspects who had committed theft in Suzhou were hiding there. Yang immediately led his team ashore for a secret investigation, capturing two suspects, Lu Abing and Luo Guansong. They were immediately taken to the team headquarters and transferred to the County Government for trial.

Suzhou

The Qian Family Robbery Suspects Escorted to Suzhou: The Qian family residence at No. 28 Enbo Lane was robbed on the 25th of last month, resulting in significant losses. The Kunshan County Detective Team arrested six bandits in Shanghai who confessed to robbing the Qian family. Zhou Hongjiang, the captain of the Wu County Public Security Bureau Detective Team, went to Shanghai to verify the facts. The six bandits have now been escorted from Shanghai to Kunshan, and the Wu County Public Security Bureau dispatched detectives to Kunshan yesterday (the 11th) to escort them back to Suzhou for trial.

Robbery Cases Emerge Frequently in Hengjing: Zhang Youqin, the head of Mufu Township in Hengjing, reported that more than ten bandits, each armed with guns, robbed his house at midnight the other day, resulting in losses of about 1,000 yuan. In addition, the Zhao Hengtai grocery store and the Zou Yongshun general store in Baoxing Town, Wangting Township, were robbed by eight bandits the night before, resulting in losses of about 100 yuan.

Nantong

Water and Land Police Jointly Suppress Pirates: Three to four hundred pirates have gathered in the Lvsi Da'an Port area, extorting and robbing merchant ships. On the 10th, the provincial and county water and land police joined forces with the Tonghaiqi Joint Defense Guerrilla Team to suppress them.

Distributing Relief to Disaster Areas in Northern Jiangsu: The National Government's Flood Relief Committee dispatched Bernard to various disaster areas along the Grand Canal in northern Jiangsu to distribute relief. For the convenience of distributing relief, Bernard commissioned the processing of American wheat into civilian flour in Nantong. It was shipped out on the 10th.

Wuxi

A Robber Caught Red-Handed at a Pawnshop: Zhou Peiyang, who runs a gluten noodle shop outside the west gate of this county, was carrying 118 silver dollars home around 8 p.m. on the evening of the 10th when he had a sudden urge to relieve himself in the Hong Taixiang alley. At that time, it was dark, and two robbers suddenly approached him and searched him, taking all the money he had on him. Zhou Peiyang shouted for help, and the police on duty nearby immediately went to pursue and arrest the robbers on the spot. The robbers, Du Jinbiao and 根长 (Gēn Cháng), refused to admit to the robbery during the preliminary hearing presided over by Chief Wang of the 4th Public Security Sub-bureau. Yesterday, a document was prepared and sent to the General Bureau for trial.

Reorganization of the County Court into a Local Branch Court: Lin Biao, the president of the Jiangsu Higher Court, decided to reorganize the county court into a local branch court, increasing the number of appellate courts to govern the preliminary appellate cases of Jiangyin, Yixing, Liyang, and Wuxi, since Wuxi is located in the center of the Beijing-Shanghai route, with developed industry and commerce, and an increasing number of civil and criminal litigation cases each year. A special order was issued to Yang, the head of this county's court, to draft a plan and budget for submission to the Ministry of Justice for review. Recently, President Lin has issued instructions from the ministry to prepare, and the head of this county's court has been instructed to prepare, with the aim of implementing the plan by March of this year at the latest. The additional expenses of more than 500 yuan per month have also been approved.

Changzhou

The Adjudication of the Mutiny Case of the Traitorous Merchants: The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association Representative Assembly previously decided on five measures regarding the mutiny case of the traitorous merchants. After the County Party Headquarters submitted them to the Provincial Party Headquarters for review, an order was received yesterday (the 10th) approving the case and instructing the county to comply. The measures decided upon are: 1) Because the mutiny case on October 18th was caused by Da Fengren's resistance to the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement, a fine of 10,000 silver dollars should be imposed on Da Fengren as a warning. The fine should be allocated to the Chamber of Commerce to cover the advanced payments; 2) From the 10,000 yuan fine imposed on Da Fengren, 9,000 yuan should be allocated as a solatium for the martyr Wu (with 1,000 yuan allocated to subsidize Wu's sister). Before Wu Wenshuang's son comes of age, only the interest can be taken, and the principal cannot be used. The remaining 1,000 yuan should be used for commemorative purposes; 3) Da Fengren is allowed to be unsealed (reopen for business). Whether Hu Ruilin instigated the mutiny case will be resolved through judicial means; 4) A letter should be sent to the County Government to execute Jin Xiangsheng, the main culprit, and to strictly arrest and bring Yu Yiqin and Jianghu Yong Zhu Yuanpei to justice.

Yangzhou

The Finance Bureau Sets a Deadline for Collecting the Busy Tax: The Jiangdu County Finance Bureau yesterday (the 9th) specially summoned the chief tax collectors of the 121 villages to urge the collection of the busy tax, setting a deadline of the end of the old lunar year to collect 150,000 yuan. The collectors requested an extension, as the amount was large and the time was short, especially after the flood. The reply was not granted. Today (the 10th), the chief secretaries have convened a general meeting and are discussing how to allocate the quotas to each village in order to report to the Finance Bureau.

The Chief of the Public Security Bureau Dismissed a Corrupt Patrol Officer: Ge Feng, the chief of the Public Security Bureau, dismissed Yi Da, a patrol officer at the Yongzhen Township Public Security Substation, for allegedly colluding with local bullies. Although more than 200 taels of opium seized on the eastern road were reported to the bureau, most of the opium was fake. The chief of the Public Security Bureau deemed this to be replacing genuine opium with fake opium and dismissed him as a punishment, transferring him to the court for handling. Xu Jun, a special agent from the bureau, was appointed to replace him.

Zhenjiang

The Fengxian Incident Transferred to the Military Department for Handling: After the Third Cavalry Division stationed in Fengxian had a mutiny, various institutions and legal bodies in the county dispatched representatives to the province and Beijing to appeal. Later, because the representatives Peng Shiheng and Dong Xueshan received a telegram from the county stating that the division commander Zhang Zhankui had asked people to mediate and requested a temporary halt to the appeal, the representatives did not go to Beijing and returned to the Provincial Government. They visited Chairman Gu, and He Haiqiao, the head of the Second Department in charge of the case, met with them, stating that the Provincial Government intended to mediate and reduce the scale of the incident, so Han Shouqian was sent to investigate and resolve the issue, but to no effect. Now, the entire case can be transferred to the Ministry of Military Affairs for handling. The representatives decided to stay in Zhenjiang and await a resolution. It is also reported that Zhang Zhankui, the division commander who caused the incident, will come to the province today to present his case to the authorities.

A Prison Warden in Yizheng Accused of Deducting Prisoners' Food: The Zhenjiang Local Court, based on a report from Kong Er and other prisoners in the Yizheng County Prison, accused the prison warden Mei Shouda of deducting prisoners' food and requested a thorough investigation. A prosecutor named Shi Zaigeng and a clerk named Wang Xia were dispatched to the county to investigate. They returned to the province yesterday after completing their duties.

Danyang

A Murder Case in the Western Countryside: Gao, the sister-in-law of Yue Shenggeng, a farmer in the western countryside, went to Qi Jia's house in Wantou Village the other night to collect membership fees but did not return overnight. The next morning, she was found dead in a nearby field with multiple knife wounds. The head of the village reported the case to the county for inspection. County Magistrate Wang, considering the seriousness of the case, immediately sent personnel to investigate. The inspection revealed that the body had no bloodstains, indicating that she was killed before being dumped. The investigation and arrest of the perpetrator are currently underway.

Gaoyou

The Zhong Family Suffers from Fire: The family of Zhong Xueshu, a farmer from Zhongjiaxia in this county, was celebrating his son's wedding the other day when sparks from the firecrackers fell into the straw pile in the back house, causing a fire. Although they tried their best to put it out, it was ineffective, and the house was burned down. The house of his cousin, Zhong Xuechang, was also affected. A total of thirty to forty houses were burned down. Because the foundation of the Zhong family's house was very high, when the dike broke, the neighbors had entrusted their valuables to the Zhong family, and everything was burned. The estimated losses are around thirty to forty thousand yuan.

A Large Number of Refugees Sent Back: After the dike broke in this county, many refugees without shelter or food went to various counties to receive relief. Now that the relief centers in various counties are closing, the refugees are returning to Gaoyou. The Gaoyou Relief Association has set up a relief center in the Confucius Temple to accommodate them. As of today, more than five hundred people have been accommodated.

Xinghua

Disaster Victims Petition to Issue County Bonds: Xinghua County has suffered frequent water and drought disasters since 1928, which have harmed the vitality of the people. This autumn, the county suffered a major flood, unprecedented in its severity. Hundreds of thousands of disaster victims rely entirely on the relief efforts of various charitable organizations to eke out a living. Now that the cold winter is coming to an end and spring plowing is approaching, it is imperative to repair dikes and purchase seeds. Therefore, disaster victims Zhang Yangqiu, Ren Daosheng, Wu Yuzhi, and others have petitioned the County Party Headquarters to convene farmers, businessmen, and legal bodies to discuss the issuance of county bonds and temporary circulating notes to provide relief.

Liuhe

Xiong Zhuangtu and His Son Accused: Huang Ziliang and other representatives of the levee residents in Baojiang Township, the Third District, accused Xiong Zhuangtu and his son (the township head) Xiong Chengtian of colluding with Yuan Han and others to collect donations per mu, damage the levee, and take soil beyond the levee boundary, and petitioned the County Government to take swift action to ensure safety. After receiving the report, County Magistrate Chen ordered the Director of the Construction Bureau and the Chief of the Third District to conduct a thorough investigation and dispatched police to arrest Yuan Hansan for interrogation.

The Flood Relief Association Sent Telegrams to Request Relief: The Liuhe Flood Relief Association held a standing committee meeting the other day to continue requesting winter and labor relief to aid the disaster victims. It also sent separate telegrams to various relief agencies to report the disaster situation and the inadequacy of labor relief, hoping for donations of relief and medicine to provide aid.

Hangzhou

Robbers from Zhuji Executed by Firing Squad: The Zhejiang Provincial Government, considering that the robbers Bi Peilin and Bi Wenquan from Zhuji had colluded with others to rob and kill Wang in Daqiaotou, were arrested and confessed during the military law trial by the Fourth Section of the Security Office. The Provincial Government approved the death sentence. Yesterday (the 11th) at 7 a.m., Zhou Wanli, an official from the Security Office, escorted the two convicts from the military prison to the scene of the crime in Zhuji and executed them by firing squad.

Local News

Minutes of the Representatives' Assembly of Various University Student Associations

The National Salvation Association of various universities in Hangzhou held its 34th Representatives' Assembly yesterday at 1:00 PM in the Law School. The schools attending were the Sino-French Medical School, Jiaotong University, Law School, Dongya University, Jinan University, Liangjiang University, Cultural University, Tongji University, Telecommunications School, Tongji Obstetrics School, Wensheng's School, Jiangnan University, Guanghua University, Zhongda Business School, Daxia University, Political Science School, Zhonggong School, Soochow University, Labor University, Tongde School, and Yixian Medical College. Li Zhiyuan of the Political Science School presided, and Tang Hansheng of the Law School recorded the minutes.

(A) Report Items:

1. Tang Hansheng of the Law School reported on the progress of negotiations with the Chamber of Commerce regarding the strike.

2. Xue Yaoting, a representative of the Shanxi Provincial Student Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, reported on the Shanxi tragedy.

(B) Discussion Items:

1. The resolution passed at the 33rd Representatives' Assembly, which called for a nationwide telegram to denounce the party and government authorities who were intentionally selling out the country, was changed to a unanimous denunciation of the government authorities who were intentionally selling out the country. The resolution was passed.

2. Two key points were established for the content of the telegram:

(1) Announce the government's crimes of harming the country and endangering the people since Japan forcibly occupied the three northeastern provinces.

(2) The people should spontaneously organize to jointly overcome national difficulties and recover lost territories. A resolution was passed, and it was entrusted to the executive committee for drafting, with a deadline of two days for issuance. The Labor University and Political Science School were designated to review it.

3. (Omitted)

4. This association will jointly organize the Shanghai Municipal Agricultural, Industrial, and Commercial Anti-Japanese National Salvation Joint Association with agricultural, industrial, and commercial organizations. It was resolved that an all-sector joint meeting would be held at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce at 2:00 PM on the 14th, convened by this association through a letter.

5. The Law School, Guanghua University, Fudan University, Political Science School, and Labor University were designated as representatives of this association to organize the all-sector joint association. It was also decided that three major missions would be proposed at the joint meeting of agriculture, industry, commerce, and students:

(1) Strikes and market shutdowns.

(2) Convening a citizens' assembly.

(3) Organizing an all-sector anti-Japanese joint association.

6. A warning to Wang Jingwei, Chiang Kai-shek, and Hu Hanmin. The resolution was handed over to the executive committee.

7. A proposed change to the fixed number of attendees for meetings of this association during the winter break. It was resolved that any school that fails to attend three consecutive meetings will have its right to attend revoked, but those who have requested leave will not be subject to this rule.

The Secondary School Student Union Holds a Representatives' Assembly

▲Telegraph Condolences to the Petition Delegation and Urge Continued Efforts

▲Request the Central Government to Punish the Shanxi Party Executive Committee

▲Warn the Fujian Provincial Government Against Acknowledging Japanese Demands

▲Request Chiang, Wang, and Hu to Go to Beijing Together to Overcome National Difficulties

There Are Three Gatherings Today

The Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association of middle school students in this city convened its 16th Representatives' Assembly at Jingye Middle School yesterday afternoon. The presidium consisted of Tu Shuang from Nanyang Middle School, Cai Ruoshan from Shanghai Middle School, and Zhang Jingsong from Huiling School. Fan Xifan from Shanghai Middle School recorded the minutes.

▲Discussion Items:

[A] Regarding the telegram from the delegation to Beijing, how should this association respond? It was resolved to send a quick mail with condolences and urge continued efforts.

[B] Proposal for this association to announce the organization of the Shanghai Municipal Industrial, Commercial, and Student Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association. It was resolved to postpone.

[C] Regarding the Shanxi provincial representative's report that the provincial and municipal party departments are suppressing the patriotic movement of the people, how should this association respond? It was resolved to telegraph the delegation to Beijing, requesting: (1) that the Central Party Department punish the executive and supervisory committee members of the Shanxi Provincial Party Department; (2) immediately arrest the fugitives and Miao Peicheng; (3) issue a declaration; (4) telegraph various sectors to jointly arrest the fugitives and Miao Peicheng.

[D] Regarding the Fujian provincial authorities' suppression of the student patriotic movement, how should this association respond? It was resolved to: (1) issue a circular telegram; (2) warn the Fujian Provincial Government; (3) telegraph the delegation to Beijing to include the following points in the petition: (a) request the government to lodge a strong protest with Japan; (b) prohibit Japanese soldiers from landing in the future; (c) reject the five conditions already accepted by the Fujian Provincial Government (i.e., the conditions put forward by Japan: (1) removal of all slogans in the city; (2) handling of student affairs by the Japanese consulate; (3) no anti-Japanese movement in Fuzhou; (4) compensation for losses; (5) apology from the Fujian Provincial Government to the Japanese consulate); (4) issue a clear order to the Fujian Provincial Government to resist to the death. (5) Since no one is responsible for the Minli Girls' Middle School, new officers should be temporarily selected to replace them. It was resolved to select Quanzhang to temporarily replace the clerical officer of Minli Girls' Middle School. (6) How should this association assist in the case of the Chengzhong Middle School authorities suppressing the students' patriotic movement? It was resolved to hand it over to the executive committee. (9) Request Chiang, Wang, and Hu to set aside personal prejudices and immediately go to Beijing together to overcome national difficulties. The resolution was passed. (10) Select another school as an economic committee. It was resolved to appoint Merun as the economic committee member. (11)(i) How should this association express itself during the delegation's visit to Beijing? It was resolved to: (a) issue a declaration; (b) notify all schools to publicize strikes and market shutdowns. (11)(ii) No resignations are allowed during the delegation's petition period. The resolution was passed. (11)(iii) If the executive committee cannot resolve the issue of the association members resuming classes, how should this association handle it? It was resolved to hand it over to the disciplinary corps. (11)(iv) The Fuyu Company in Fuzhou was leased to the violent Japanese by treacherous merchants, who will use this to seize Fujian Province. How should this association assist? It was resolved to hand over the assistance plan to the executive committee. The meeting adjourned after the discussions. It was also reported that the association has scheduled a meeting of the disciplinary corps at Jingye Middle School at 1:00 PM this afternoon, and representatives from various schools are expected to attend on time. At the same time (1:00 PM this afternoon), the preparatory committee for costumed propaganda will meet at the office at 15 Jiping Lane. Representatives are requested to attend on time. It was also heard that the meeting of the Japanese goods inspection committee, originally scheduled for 2:00 PM this afternoon, slightly conflicts with the time of the representatives' assembly, so it will be held at 4:00 PM this afternoon.

[P Feng Huanzhang Lectures at Provincial Shanghai Middle School >

Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, Provincial Shanghai Middle School held a graduation ceremony for the spring class of the third grade in the auditorium of the junior high school department. Feng Huanrong was invited to give a lecture. Guests Jiang Wenyu, Ren Zhongmin, and others, as well as teachers and students of the school, totaling over a hundred people, attended. After the formal ceremony, the current principal of the school delivered the opening address, followed by Feng's lecture. The main points were as follows: (1) Stating that our country is now in extreme danger, and the land and property left to us by our ancestors are being occupied by powerful enemies. We, as descendants, cannot preserve them. This is shameful and disgraceful. (2) Although our enemy is strong, we cannot give up resisting him because of his power. We must strive for survival under oppression and must fight and resist our enemies. (3) Youth is the vitality of the country. If we want our country to become strong in the future and our people to be relieved of suffering, we must rely on the patriotic youth who are knowledgeable, ambitious, full of spirit and determination to unite and generate a true force for resisting Japan and saving the country. Only then will the country have hope. Subsequently, diplomas were issued, and guests Ren Zhongmin, teacher representative Shen Yizhen, and student representative Tang Dunye gave speeches successively. Finally, graduate Wang Zhian gave a response.

The Education Bureau Approves the Registration of Nanyang Commercial School

Nanyang Commercial Senior High School was founded in the ninth year of the Republic and has a history of twelve years. It currently has over 600 students in both the male and female divisions. Since Wu Xinglian, the principal of the school, returned to Shanghai from the United States last year, he has implemented the purchase of school buildings on Tongji Road and has also carried out registration procedures. Yesterday, the school received instructions from the Municipal Education Bureau, stating that the school's operations are satisfactory and that its registration has been approved.

Sports

Jinan Avenges Previous Defeat, Malaya Suffers Another Loss

▲Two to Zero Overall Dullness

▲Second Half No Winner

Malaya Will Fight the British Army Team Tomorrow

The Malayan Overseas Chinese Football Team lost again to Jinan University yesterday by a score of two to zero at the China Baseball Field. Three to four thousand people watched. After the fierce battle against Donghua on Sunday, they were somewhat affected. When the Malayans came to Shanghai last time, they won 3-0. Jinan returned the favor with a 2-0 victory. The crowd hoped Jinan would avenge their previous defeat. Yesterday's situation was completely in favor of Jinan. In the first half, Chen Zhenhe and Qiu Dongyan each scored a goal. In the second half, Chen and Qiu were injured and left the field. There were also injuries on the Malayan side. As a result, the situation became even more dull. The referee was Jiang Xiangqing. Tomorrow afternoon, Malaya will play against the British Army United Team at the same location.

▲Jinan Lineup

Chen Buzhang, Gu Shangquan, Jiang Shanjing, Liang Shutang, Feng Yunyou, Chen Fuzhong, Fu Hexuan, Qiu Dongyan, Jiang Zongmian, Chen Zhenhe (out), Yang Baosen, Wen Dingxin (out), Mei Hongshi

▲Malaya Lineup

Huang Jinbai, Xu Jintang, Yu Zhuohou, Gan Jinlu, Jian Deyao, Huang Kehou, Liu Jinrong, Guan Xinnian, Xie Jinfu, Deng Yueyun, Xia Haishan

▲Dull Situation

Malaya remained subjugated throughout the game. The opportunities for the forwards to get the ball were extremely rare. In the first half, Jinan besieged the Malayan goal from time to time. In the second half, Jinan replaced Chen Zhenhe and Qiu Dongyan due to injuries, giving Malaya a chance to recover. Both sides made aimless attacks in the end, resulting in a dull game.

▲Goalkeeping Spotlight

In this situation, the goalkeeper was the most prominent player. Malayan goalkeeper Huang Jinbai, accepting his fate, pounced up and down, rushing forward and defending backward. His performance was indeed solid and was praised by the audience, who called him the "Iron Gate," which was well-deserved.

▲Weak Midfield

Malaya's defeat was influenced by the cold weather, which greatly reduced their activity. However, the weakness of the midfield line cannot be ignored, allowing the enemy to approach from both sides. The inability of the midfielders to support the forwards and the lack of coordination among the forwards, as well as the lack of direction in passing the ball, were all major problems that affected their strength.

▲Jinan's Pressure

Jinan controlled the entire game and was very pleased with themselves. The changes in the midfield and defense did not affect their strength. Gu Shangquan's defense was steady and reliable. Feng Yunyou's midfield also attacked the goal many times, showing great potential. The Malayan goalkeeper, Zhang, made many saves, but Jinan could have won by a wider margin if they had scored on more opportunities. All the Jinan players performed very well.

▲Chen and Qiu Score Consecutively

Jinan dared to attack as soon as they got the ball. They approached the city walls again and again, but were repeatedly blocked by the iron gate. Ten minutes into the game, Mei Hongmai advanced straight on the right side, approaching the right corner, and hooked the ball into the middle. Chen Zhenhe was about to attack the goal, but Malayan left-back Xu Jintang saw the situation was not good and cleared the ball out of bounds. Fu Hefeng's corner kick was excellent. Chen Zhenhe followed the momentum and shot a flat ball downward from five yards to the left of the goal. The ball was too powerful. Huang Jinbai squatted down, caught it, but still bounced into the corner of the goal, giving Jinan a 1-0 lead. Ten minutes later, Qiu Dongyan shot from fifteen yards away, right in the center, breaking through the goal again. Jinan won the first half with a score of 2-0.

▲Key Players Injured

The second half was similar, but five minutes into the game, Chen Zhenhe injured his leg and could not continue. Jiang Zongmian replaced him, which was not as effective. As a result, Malaya saw a chance to recover. Jinan proceeded cautiously. Then, Huang Jinbai repeatedly made dangerous saves, maintaining the original score. Almost half an hour later, Qiu Dongyan also injured his foot and left the field. Jinan did not replace him, continuing the game with ten players. Malaya also ended up playing with only ten players.

▲Battle Against the British Army

Tomorrow afternoon at 3:00 PM, Malaya will play against the Shanghai British Army United Team at the same location. The situation is different, and the Malayan athletes are still expected to work hard.
