Local News II

Japanese Yarn Falsely Marked with Chinese Merchant Labels

▲A Cunning Plan to Change Appearances

▲Rong Zongjing Sends People to Investigate and Seize the Goods

Since the Mukden Incident, and the exposure of Japan's plot to invade the Eastern Provinces, the Chinese people have been motivated by righteous indignation to engage in an economic boycott of Japan. Everyone has been calling for action, and the whole country is united. As a result, Japanese trade in China has suffered a major blow, especially the yarn industry. Unexpectedly, recently in Shanghai, there have been shameless merchants who privately purchased Japanese yarn, changed its appearance, and falsely used the trademarks of famous Chinese yarn factories, passing off the bad for the good in order to make a large profit. Yesterday at midnight, employees of the Shen Xin Yarn Factory received a tip and seized 15 large packages of Japanese yarn in Pudong that were falsely marked with the factory's "Man Bell" trademark. The details of the incident are as follows:

▲Rong's Yarn Business: Mr. Rong Zongjing, a wealthy merchant from Wuxi, is a giant in the Chinese flour industry and also holds the reins of the yarn and cotton industry. The most famous Shen Xin Yarn Factory in Shanghai was founded by Mr. Rong. There are a total of nine Shen Xin factories established one after another. Except for the third factory located in Wuxi and the fourth factory located in Hankou, the remaining seven factories (numbers 1, 2, 5, 6, 7, 8, and 9) are all located in the Pudong area of Shanghai. Their scale is enormous, unmatched by other factories. Their products are of excellent quality and their reputation is well-established.

Photograph of the seized counterfeit cotton yarn

▲Dishonest Merchants Counterfeit Brands: Since the September 18th Incident and the subsequent economic boycott of Japan, Japanese yarn prices have plummeted. Mr. Rong took advantage of this opportunity to increase production day and night to meet the urgent demand. Unexpectedly, two weeks ago, Mr. Rong received a report that unscrupulous merchants were secretly replacing the trademarks on Japanese yarn with those of Chinese yarn factories, changing its appearance and falsely using the Shen Xin "20-count Yellow Man Bell" and "42-count Blue Man Bell" brands, selling them on the market. He was asked to immediately conduct a thorough investigation to deter such wrongdoing.

▲Dispatching Men to Track Down the Source: Upon hearing the report, Mr. Rong paid special attention and immediately secretly instructed Hu Qingsheng, the director of general affairs of the Fifth Factory, and Qi Haitian, the chief inspector, to be responsible for the investigation. Hu and Qi immediately dispatched several staff members to investigate in various places, but with little success. It wasn't until the morning of the 9th that a secret informant came forward, saying that he had recently seen trucks from the Japanese shipping company Rikuun Kaisha near Kunming Road. There were traces of yarn on the trucks, which looked suspicious. Hu and Qi immediately drove to the location. When they arrived at the middle section of Kunming Road, they saw trucks from Rikuun Kaisha (numbers 1428 and 16513) and a truck from the Shanghai Moving Company (number 9720 in the Concession) parked there. The trucks were loaded with Japanese yarn, and several workers were moving the yarn into a new-style bungalow at number 184.

▲Waiting Patiently to Seize the Opportunity: Hu and Qi became suspicious of the situation. Since the bungalow at number 184 was neither a warehouse nor a weaving factory, there was no doubt that there was some secret activity going on. Hu and Qi secretly discussed how to proceed. Hu returned to the factory to report, while Qi remained on Kunming Road to secretly monitor the situation. They waited patiently for two days and two nights. Finally, at 7:05 AM yesterday morning, they saw two trucks, fully loaded with cotton yarn, drive out. Hu and Qi remained calm and followed behind in a car. They followed the trucks all the way to the intersection of Tiantong Road and Disiwei Road in Zhabei, which is under the jurisdiction of the Fifth District, Third Precinct of the Public Security Bureau.

▲Calling the Police to Solve the Case: At that time, someone on the truck at the rear noticed the car that Hu and Qi were in and was about to try to escape. Hu and Qi got out of their car and signaled to the police to stop the two trucks. Upon closer inspection of the yarn, it was clearly Japanese "20-count Hoynen" brand yarn that had been relabeled as Shen Xin "Yellow Man Bell" and Japanese "42-count Blue Phoenix" brand yarn that had been falsely marked as Shen Xin "42-count Blue Man Bell." They were taken to the Fifth District, Third Precinct. After questioning by Chief Zhang, the driver of the truck, Wang Guixun, from Ningbo, confessed that the Japanese yarn was loaded from the Toyota Yarn Factory, transported to number 184 Kunming Road, and relabeled. Today, under the orders of a Japanese man named Mori, he was transporting the counterfeit yarn to the Japanese disinfection facility on Disiwei Road for packaging, and then transporting it to other ports for sale. As for Shanghai, the Huachang Dyeing and Weaving Factory on Fulili Road in the French Concession was acting as a consignment agent.

▲Japanese People Dejected and Leave: While Chief Zhang was conducting the preliminary hearing, Japanese people including Yamaji, Kimura, and Mita led a large group of Japanese ruffians to the police station, shouting loudly and behaving aggressively. Seeing the situation was not good, Chief Zhang feared that an accident would occur. He tried to appease the Japanese with words while urgently telegraphing the headquarters for instructions. When Director Wen heard the news, he immediately dispatched Director Hong of the Foreign Affairs Section of the Second Division to negotiate. When Hong arrived at the Fifth District, the Japanese ruffians were still gathered at the gate of the police station. After Hong sternly rebuked them, the Japanese were at a loss for words and had no room for argument. They left dejectedly. Director Hong also hurried back to report to Director Wen.

▲Transfer to the Court: After hearing Director Hong's report, Director Wen decided that since both parties resided in the International Settlement, the case should be transferred to the court for legal proceedings. He ordered Chief Zhang to first count the total number of packages on the two trucks, which was 64 large bales. He then notified the Harbin Police Station to send the original goods and the driver to the First Special District Court to be handled by Judge Zhou. Judge Zhou deemed it necessary to investigate the case and immediately sent both parties to the Yangshupu Police Station for investigation. The driver, Wang Guixun, was temporarily detained for questioning. The Shen Xin employees, Hu and Qi, were ordered to temporarily return to the factory and await the trial.

Hu Yongchang Company Secretly Imports Large Quantities of Japanese Coal

▲The Trade Association Voluntarily Reports the Offense

▲The Municipal Anti-Japanese Association Investigates, Determines the Facts, and Confiscates the Goods

According to the China News Agency, the Shanghai Coal Trade Association formed a Japanese goods inspection team after Japan invaded and occupied the Northeast. They have been working hard on inspection work. Recently, with the fall of Jinzhou and the increasingly precarious national situation, the association's work has become even more intense. At 9:00 AM yesterday (the 11th), inspectors from the association discovered a Japanese Mitsui coal ship near Hengfeng Bridge on the Suzhou Creek. After investigation, it was confirmed that it was purchased from the Japanese Mitsui Yoko by the Hu Yongchang Coal Company of Chihang Bridge, Xinza Road, with more than 200 tons of coal on board. The ship had just sailed from the new Mitsui Yoko warehouse in Pudong and had already unloaded 30 tons. The owner of the company, Hu Jifu, recklessly undermined the anti-Japanese goods movement and, under the pretext of the Concession's power, requested the Xinza Road Police Station to send officers to escort the Japanese coal ashore. The inspectors from the Coal Trade Association reported this to the inspection department of the Municipal Anti-Japanese Association, which dispatched personnel to intervene, detain the ship, and transport the remaining ten tons of Japanese coal to the Yitaixing West Warehouse on Guangfu Road in Zhabei. According to coal industry insiders, Hu Jifu, the owner of the Hu Yongchang Coal Company, usually sang high praises for patriotism and boycotting Japanese goods in the association, but secretly engaged in this despicable behavior. American Woman Crowley Imprisoned for Smuggling Opium

▲First Opium Case Handled by the U.S. Court for China

According to the Great American Evening Post, American woman Crowley, who is known for importing ice cream to China for sale, was arrested at her residence in the French Concession at 8:30 PM on Saturday night by the U.S. Deputy Marshal, two assistants, and French Concession police officers. Because the case is serious, bail was set at US$10,000. The bail has not yet been paid, so she remains in custody. Crowley is charged with smuggling opium. The indictment was filed by U.S. Attorney Selette, who claims that Crowley, between August 11 and September 13 of last year, smuggled 55 tins of opium, each tin containing three to four ounces of opium, from Shanghai to an unspecified port in the Pacific Ocean aboard the U.S. Navy destroyer USS Chaumont. The case was discovered through the collaborative investigation efforts of U.S. authorities in Shanghai and the U.S. Department of Justice and Treasury personnel stationed on the Pacific coast. This is the first time in the history of the U.S. Court for China that an American has been charged with smuggling opium. U.S. Judge Pandy has subpoenaed witnesses from Germany, and the trial will begin as soon as they arrive in Shanghai. The details of the smuggling are still unknown. However, it is reported that there was an accomplice on board the USS Chaumont. It is worth noting that Crowley was charged with running a brothel in Harbin in 1923 and was fined US$500 by the U.S. Judge. In 1930, she was fined US$50 for assault.

Merchants and Residents of Nanshi Petition for Tax Reduction

▲Notification Slips Affixed with Tax Stamps

▲Heavy Burden and Trouble

More than one hundred merchants and residents in the area of Nanshi's Nine Mu Land recently contacted the Shanghai Precious Tax Bureau, arguing that the requirement for all shops to affix tax stamps to notification slips was an excessive burden and troublesome procedure. They pointed out that even a minor oversight in affixing the stamps would result in severe penalties, causing them considerable distress. Yesterday, they organized a group of more than one hundred merchants and residents and sent two representatives, Chen Huikang and Zhang Shengkang, to the Bureau at Xiaoximen to request an exemption. The Director of the Shanghai Precious Tax Bureau, Song Ziju, was not present at the time, so the representatives were received by a staff member named Yi Mingshang. The representatives stated their purpose and requested an exemption from the tax stamp requirement for notification slips to ease the burden on merchants and residents. However, Yi stated that the requirement to affix tax stamps to notification slips was stipulated by the national government's stamp tax law. He said that he had no authority to grant an exemption and that it would affect central regulations. He indicated that he could not be responsible for the merchants and residents' request. Negotiations continued for a long time, and by 1:00 PM, there was still no resolution. The merchants and residents then returned in an orderly manner.

Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Opposes the Municipal Council's High Assessment of Rent

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce issued a declaration regarding the Public Concession Municipal Council's high assessment of rent and collection of general taxes: The Shanghai Municipal Council's method of collecting general taxes, except for self-occupied properties that require rent assessment, follows financial principles and uses the actual rent as the calculation standard. Recently, it has come up with an unconventional idea to inflate rents as a step towards increasing taxes. For example, actual rents of 84 taels per month are being assessed at 190 taels. In essence, this is no different from increasing the tax rate from 14% to over 28%. In the past, whenever the Municipal Council increased tax rates, this Association, acting in the interests of taxpayers, invariably expressed opposition. Even the extra two-percent tax that started in the autumn of 1927 was only cancelled last autumn after strenuous efforts. Since the Municipal Council realizes that a straightforward increase is difficult and a unified increase is inconvenient, it is resorting to a strategy of divide and conquer, using a sleight of hand. If we do not strenuously oppose this, allowing it to undermine the fundamental principles of finance and the established practice of the past sixty years, then in the future, the tax rate may remain unchanged, but inflating rents will be enough to satisfy its desire to extract more revenue. How can taxpayers bear this ever-increasing burden? We hereby issue this declaration for public awareness. January 11, 1932.

Ministry of Interior Approves Temporary Suspension of Dance Hall Ban in Shanghai

▲Requesting Municipal Government to Determine a Deadline

▲Municipal Government Instructs Public Security Bureau to Review and Reply

On October 20th, the Municipal Government received a communication from the Ministry of Interior regarding the Central Executive Committee's resolution to ban commercial dance halls nationwide to promote social morality. The Municipal Government was instructed to implement the ban in Shanghai. Subsequently, various dance halls in the city, both Chinese and foreign-owned, jointly submitted a petition requesting the Municipal Government to temporarily suspend the ban. The Municipal Government considered that the reasons presented by the dance halls were somewhat justifiable and forwarded the petition to the Ministry of Interior for review on December 19th. It has now been learned that the Municipal Government has recently received a reply from the Ministry of Interior stating that since Shanghai has special circumstances, the request for a temporary suspension of the ban should be approved. However, the Ministry requested the Shanghai Municipal Government to investigate the local situation, determine a deadline, and report back for record-keeping. Upon receiving the communication, the Municipal Government has instructed the Public Security Bureau to comply with the instructions, propose a deadline, and submit a report for review.

Public and Social Affairs Bureaus Thoroughly Investigate Labor Unrest at Three Japanese Factories in Western Shanghai

The workers at the Japanese-owned Rihua Textile Factory, Kiwa Textile Factory, and Toyo Silk Factory in Western Shanghai went on strike due to oppression by the Japanese management. In order to quickly resolve the issue, Public Security Bureau Director Wen Yingxing and Social Affairs Bureau Director Mai Zhaoshu specially dispatched Zhang Shouchun, Wang Bing, Zhu Jintao, Li Hua, and others to conduct a thorough investigation to facilitate mediation.

Abnormal Weather

▲Heavy Fog, Winter Feels Like Spring

Shanghai has experienced several days of heavy fog. The fog was even denser yesterday morning. As dawn approached, the fog was so thick that it was difficult to recognize people even a few steps away. The streetcars were also moving slowly. It wasn't until after 7:00 AM that the clouds cleared and the sun shone through. However, the weather felt like spring.

Minutes of the General Meeting of the Sino-French Alumni Association

On January 10, 1932, at noon, the Sino-French School Alumni Association held its sixth annual general meeting at the Atlantic Restaurant on Fourth Avenue to re-elect executive committee members and supervisors. A total of more than 60 members attended, including Zhang Wenbin, Zhou Guisheng, Hu Fangjin, Ma Jieren, and Song Youfan. Zhang Wenbin presided over the meeting, and Lin Jun served as the secretary. The following matters were reported: (1) The Chairman's report: The Chairman stated that the attendance of members today was very enthusiastic, and he was very pleased that most of the professors from the alma mater had come to participate. He said that the work of the association in the past year had been smooth and that the financial situation was stable due to the subsidy from the French Public Works Bureau. He expressed optimism about the future of the association and hoped that alumni would visit the association from time to time to offer their guidance. (2) Chen Boping reported on the work of the Documentation Section over the past year. (3) Xie Xuefang reported on the financial situation for the year 1931. Matters for discussion: (A) Yan Shishu proposed a motion to reduce membership fees and waive membership fees for unemployed members. After detailed discussion, the motion to reduce membership fees was temporarily deemed difficult to implement. The motion to waive membership fees for unemployed members was passed. (B) Lin Jun proposed a motion to expand recruitment of members, which was unanimously approved. (C) Gao Songnian proposed that the Alumni Association should provide an opinion box so that members could submit opinions on reforming the association's affairs at any time. This was approved. (D) Hu Guocheng proposed whether the method of awarding scholarships from the alma mater could be changed so that cash rewards would not be used. After discussion, it was decided that graduating students should be invited to attend each annual general meeting in the future to strengthen connections. (E) The Accounting Section submitted the revenue and expenditure budget for the year 1932, which was unanimously approved. Due to the tight financial situation, it was decided that (1) the quarterly magazine would be changed to a semi-annual publication, (2) efforts would be made to exchange the billiard table when necessary, and (3) the amount of the deficit would be compensated by one year's interest from the 1931 fund. The election results were announced: Zhang Wenbin, Lin Jun, Zhang Chunsheng, Hu Guocheng, Lu Kunshui, Xie Xuefang, Zhou Shengbo, Chen Boping, Shen Zhongjun, Ren Wenzhen, Shi Hongsheng, Dai Chunfeng, Gong Shifu, Song Chaogang, and Guo Zhongliang were elected as executive committee members. Gao Songnian, Gan Yucan, Ma Jieren, and Ding Hongji were elected as alternate executive committee members. Hu Fangjin, Fang Shengping, Fei Xizhen, Zhu Kongjia, and Hu Fangming were elected as supervisors. You Peisheng and Zhou Guisheng were elected as alternate supervisors. The meeting adjourned at 4:00 PM.

Naughty Boy Hanging Onto a Streetcar Has His Right Leg Crushed

Recently, there have been many cases of naughty children chasing streetcars in the middle of the road and hanging onto the iron fences with both hands (commonly known as "hanging onto the streetcar"). By the time the ticket collector notices them, they have already jumped off, which is extremely dangerous. Yesterday at noon, a boy named Shen Zhuting (11 years old) was chasing a French fifth-route streetcar near North Zhejiang Road and Eyre Road. He accidentally slipped and fell to the ground, and his right leg was caught under the wheel and crushed. His flesh was mangled, and he lost consciousness. The police arrived, recorded the driver's badge number 171, hired a car to take the child to the hospital, but he died soon after.

Opium Seized in a Car

Yesterday morning at about 3:15, West Police Officer No. 331 and Chinese Police Officer No. 327 of the Jing'an Temple Police Station were patrolling near Xiaoshadu Road and Avenue Haig and saw a car driving by, which looked suspicious. They stopped the car and searched it. They found a large package of opium weighing about 24 pounds in the car, and three jars of opium paste in a basket. They took the passenger Huang Rongsheng and the driver Hou Fugen to the police station for investigation. The license plate number of the car they were in was 780.

Cui Tang Gave Birth to Triplets

Cui Baoyuan, a worker at the Songchun Sauce Garden on Western Shanghai's Bailinan Road, is from Haiyan, Zhejiang. He married Tang last year in his hometown and then brought her to Shanghai. They lived in the nearby Kangjiaqiao, at No. 6, Duoduo Lane, next to the Shenyuan Dog Racing Track. Cui was not often home. Tang, who was six months pregnant, has been pregnant for about a year. Yesterday morning, Tang suddenly had severe abdominal pain. Cui realized she was about to give birth and quickly hired a midwife, Zhang Kang, to come to the house. Soon after, Tang gave birth. Unexpectedly, she gave birth to two babies. The family thought they were twins and did not pay much attention. However, the mother's abdomen did not shrink and she was still in severe pain. The midwife examined her and found that there was still something in her womb and that the placenta had not yet come out. After the midwife applied her skills, another child was born. All three children were boys, and they were quite strong. The neighborhood was in an uproar, and everyone came to watch.

Record of Newly Elected Officers of the Lianqing Society

The Lianqing Society was founded by the renowned American-educated Li Yuanxin and has existed for more than eight years. There are more than 80 members, all of whom are major merchants in Shanghai and graduates from Europe and the United States. The new officers for this year have been elected recently. The president is Li Yuanxin, who has been re-elected for the third year. The vice presidents are Wu Shougong and Ma Bole. The treasurer is Xu Zhendong. The secretary is Liu Congqiang. The new directors are Xu Naili, Shen Siliang, Chen Liting, Li Shuming, and Wang Zhiren.

Central Bank Inspection Report

▲113th Inspection

The 113th Inspection Report on the Issuance Reserve of the Central Bank states: This Committee is responsible for inspecting the reserve for the issuance of convertible notes of the Central Bank in accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations. The 113th inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of the Bank on January 9, 1932. The results of the inspection are announced as follows: (A) The total amount of convertible notes issued is 29,831,539 silver yuan, including 27,144,749 silver yuan notes and 2,686,790 subsidiary notes. The total amount of the convertible note reserve is 29,831,539 silver yuan, including cash reserve of 23,453,539 silver yuan. The cash reserve is deposited in the issuing vault of this bank, 19,717,524.45 silver yuan, in branch banks in various ports, 2,029,829 silver yuan, and in other banks, 1,700,6185.55 silver yuan. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 6,378,000 silver yuan. (B) Regarding the total issuance of convertible notes of 250,000 yuan, the total reserve for关金 convertible notes is 250,000 yuan. The reserve includes US$100,000 deposited in local banks, converted to关金 at a fixed price of 40. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's Convertible Note Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%, which is in compliance with the regulations. This report is hereby submitted. January 9, 1932, Li Fuxun, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Supervisors Yu Qiaqing, Bei Songsun, Wang Jingli, Qi Runqing, Hu Mengjia, and Tang Shoumin.

Robbery on Miller Road

At about 8:00 PM last night, six robbers broke into No. 617 Miller Road in Hongkou. Two of them were armed with pistols and forbade anyone from making a sound. As a result, clothing and jewelry were robbed, estimated to be worth over 200 yuan. When they left, they fired several shots. They were chased by the neighborhood security team, who captured one robber on the spot and confiscated a pistol. The robber was taken to the police station for investigation.

Law Weekly Published

Law Weekly, edited by He Jia and with Xu Yuandao as the chief editor, is a good reading material for domestic scholars studying law. The contributors are all legal scholars from home and abroad. There are also many translated texts. There are 52 issues per year, and it is not sold retail. The subscription address is Xin Shehui Bookstore, No. 105 Chuanshi Highway, Beishi. The first issue is about to be published.

Zhenyi and Huangdu Post Offices

Collect Payment and Insured Packages

According to the Shanghai Post Office, Zhenyi and Huangdu Post Offices began accepting domestic collect payment and insured packages on December 16 of last year. The amount of collect payment and insurance is limited to 500 yuan.

News from the Electrical Research Association

In view of the fact that radio science is still in its infancy in China, the Shanghai Chinese Electrical Experimentation Research Association, considering that most of the various components are manufactured abroad and there are few domestic inventions, which is regrettable, Chen Shan, a member of the association, has been diligently researching and has invented a substitute for the B-type motor. After testing by the association's research department, the results are quite satisfactory. The substitute B-type motor is an important component in radio, and this is the first contribution to the Chinese electrical industry.

All Sectors Should be Aware of Those Who Use Counterfeit Money to Swindle

Recently, it has been discovered that three Chinese people are in the habit of using one-yuan, five-yuan, and ten-yuan counterfeit banknotes to swindle. Their method is usually to pretend to buy clothes in clothing stores, and take the opportunity to mix the counterfeit money in with the real money. The appearances and clothing of the three men are as follows: (1) About 25 or 26 years old, about 5 feet 5 inches tall, black face with pockmarks, wearing a brown long gown and a felt hat, often shaking his shoulders when walking. (2) About 25 years old, 5 feet 5 inches tall, long face and yellow skin, wearing a black long gown and a black leather hat. (3) About 22 years old, about 5 feet 2 inches tall, long face and yellow skin, wearing a blue cotton gown and a felt hat. All three speak the Shanghai dialect.

Graduation and Certificate Awarding Ceremony for Nurses at Pushan Hospital

The obstetrics department of Zhabei Pushan Hospital provides daily medical treatment and medicine, benefiting the common people considerably. The hospital has daily courses to teach medical knowledge to nurses, so as to cultivate talents. On New Year's Eve last year, the first class of nurses from the hospital graduated. The medical director, Mr. Shi Yixuan, invited the hospital director, Wang Yiting, and directors Chen Liangyu and Wang Junsheng to the hospital to hold the certificate awarding ceremony and deliver speeches.

Case Against the Head of the First District of the County Concluded

▲ Court Rules No Prosecution

Wu Jingqing, the head of the Minhang District, the first district of Shanghai County, was previously accused by villagers Feng Jingming and others of dereliction of duty and other crimes in the local court. After two court hearings by Prosecutor Zhao of the court, it is now known that the court believes that the three points alleged by the plaintiff have no definite evidence to offer. The case has been investigated in accordance with the law and it is considered that a decision of no prosecution should be made. Yesterday, the decision of no prosecution was sent to the police to be delivered to Wu Quwei and others for receipt.

New Year's Issue of Real Estate Monthly Published

The Shanghai Real Estate Monthly New Year's issue, compiled and printed by the Puben Real Estate Company in this city, has been published. In addition to publishing a summary of business operations in December of last year, it also includes important topics such as real estate business methods and a glimpse into land law. It is of great benefit to real estate owners and those who intend to engage in real estate business. As the new year approaches, anyone who wants to acquire property or design and build should have a copy. The excellence of the printing and the thoroughness of the compilation are especially noteworthy. Free copies are available to all sectors upon request, but detailed name, address, and occupation must be provided.

News from the Jiande Society's Persuasion Meeting

The Zhonghua Jiande Society on Laobaizi Road and Fusheng Road in this city has been established for twelve years. Its purpose has always been very pure. Since the construction of a five-story spacious clubhouse, the foundation has been solid. After reorganization in July of last year, Mr. Wang Xiaoxu took over as president and appointed Mr. Wang Chengdian as director-general, actively rectifying everything, so the society's affairs are thriving. In view of the recent natural and man-made disasters and repeated foreign troubles, the society has spared no effort in carrying out all anti-Japanese and national salvation work, such as raising relief funds, distributing cotton clothes, organizing patriotic volunteer armies, and anti-Japanese costumed propaganda teams, all of which have achieved considerable results. However, the society believes that it is difficult to achieve results in running public welfare undertakings without concentrating talents and cooperating together. Therefore, without avoiding danger, it resolutely held the tenth membership persuasion meeting during this period of national crisis, formed teams to solicit new comrades to join, and Mr. Wang Xiaolai served as the commander of the team, and enthusiastic people from all walks of life served as the captains of the branch teams to carry out the work. The society has printed detailed regulations and various printed materials, stating the various benefits of joining the society, for all sectors to request, aspire to join, and it is also heard that the society, in order to increase interest in the society and promote the movement for thrift and integrity, holds a motivational meeting at the society every two weeks. The day before yesterday morning was the day of the second meeting. The program included a warning drama [Jian Jian] by the society's Propaganda Department and Peking Opera by the Peking Opera Department. More than 800 members attended, which was quite a grand occasion.

Miracle Drug for Frostbite Arrives in Shanghai

Frostbite has always had no good medicine, but the HoPse frostbite medicine of the Jian Er Zi brand issued by the New Yihe Company works miraculously in a day. In order to prove the miraculous effect, the company will send a box of the medicine to any patient who writes to No. 5 Zunde Lane, Zhejiang Road, and only collect the medicine cost after the patient is cured. It is also heard that Sincere Company and Jihuatang Pharmacy on Xuenan Road are also selling it.

Bandit Jiang Zuohui Imprisoned for Three Years and Six Months

The bandit Jiang Zuohui, in December of last year, together with the fugitives Hu Axiang, Sanbao, Amao, and Four People, held weapons and broke into the cigarette and paper shop opened by Xu Juliang at No. 35 Pingjili Road in the French Concession to commit robbery. At that time, fortunately, Xu's wife saw the situation and cleverly turned off the light switch, and the whole shop was dark. Jiang and the bandits had no time to commit robbery, turned around and rushed out of the door to escape. The shop also blew the police whistle to warn. The Yue patrolman on duty nearby heard the sound and rushed to pursue. Jiang held a gun and tried to open fire to resist arrest. The Yue patrolman quickly drew his gun and returned fire, wounding Jiang's leg and knocking him to the ground. He was captured and a pistol was seized. The other bandits had already escaped without a trace. He was taken to the police station. The police chief ordered him to be sent to the hospital for treatment. Now that he has recovered, he has been taken back to the police station by the detective and sent to the Second Special Court for investigation and detention. After investigation and verification, he was summoned again yesterday. Police lawyer Chen Ming explained the case and prosecuted him for the crime of robbery by a gang of three or more people carrying weapons under the criminal law. The victim Xu Juliang also testified about the situation of the defendant and others coming to rob. Jiang confessed that he was forced to go to rob by the fugitive Hu Axiang. After the court appointed lawyer Xu Yannian as the defendant's pro bono defense, Judge Xiong announced the end of the trial and sentenced Jiang Zuohui on the spot to three years and six months of imprisonment for the crime of robbery by a gang of three or more people carrying weapons. The number of days of detention before the judgment is final shall be offset against the sentence at a rate of two days for one day. The pistol was confiscated.

Recent Developments in the Diagnosis and Treatment at Jisheng Hospital

Jisheng Hospital, located at No. 110 East Pushishi Road in the French Concession, was founded by Dr. Wang Zhenchuan and is quite grand in scale. The hospital's main purpose is charity, and it specially invites doctors Wang Peiyuan, Hou Guangdi, Zhou Hongzhang, Zhang Danqing, and Chen Jingfang to take turns providing voluntary diagnosis and treatment services every day, dispensing medicine, and benefiting the poor considerably. There is also a separate department for quitting smoking. Regardless of the severity of the smoking addiction, whether quitting while walking or quitting while staying, addiction can be broken in a month.

Fire in a Thatched House on Tianbao Road

A thatched house at a certain number on Tianbao Road, Hujia Muqiao, Zhabei, where Zhu Risheng (60 years old) from Yancheng lived, caught fire at 2:20 p.m. yesterday due to playing with matches. Immediately, smoke filled the air and became uncontrollable, spreading to 37 adjacent thatched houses. Later, the Zhabei Fire Brigade drove pump trucks to the scene and worked hard to put out the fire, which was extinguished until after 5 p.m.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 p.m. yesterday said that the weather is sunny and colder, and there are foggy areas in the Yangtze River basin and along the coast here. Bohai is cloudy with snow. A new cyclone has risen around Shandong due to the Mongolian low pressure moving westward. The wind along the coast south of Ma'an Island is directionless. Also, in the 24 hours before 3 p.m. yesterday, the temperature in this city was 60 degrees at its highest and 32.2 degrees at its lowest. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 27.3 degrees and the lowest was 13.8 degrees.

Reader Correspondence

The Path to Be Taken by the Youth National Salvation Movement Wang Le Yi

Now Jinzhou has fallen, and the Eastern Provinces have been lost. What is the responsibility we bear, and what is the mission we hold? The soldiers advocate the suicidal policy of [non-resistance], which is of course not to be discussed. Even the current national patriotic movement of the youth is mostly going in the wrong direction. They all abandon their studies with a momentary impulsive passion, and run around shouting. If that is not enough, they follow it up with hunger strikes, suicides, or going to the front line to kill the enemy. However, the survival of a country is no more than the collection of three elements: intelligence, military strength, and financial resources. China has millions of soldiers, so it cannot be said that its military strength is not strong. It has vast and fertile land, so it cannot be said that its financial resources are not rich. However, why can't China dominate the world, and even dare not fight Japan, and is in danger of becoming a subjugated slave? This is because its intelligence is inferior to others. Youth is the life force of the nation, the lifeline of the country, and the spirit of society. Now, to make such a meaningless sacrifice, isn't it painful? Isn't it worrying? Some people say [The anti-Japanese work done by young people now is not a national salvation movement, but a national subjugation movement.] Whether this kind of bad evaluation is credible or not, let's ignore it for now, but let us ask ourselves, are we going in the wrong direction and recognizing the wrong goal? Students, please think carefully. Japan was originally a poor and weak country and an oppressed nation, but why is it now so strong and able to dominate the world? Because after the Meiji Restoration, it was able to painstakingly study science and education, and strive to reform social organization and national politics. During the Franco-Prussian War, France was defeated by Prussia, ceded land and paid reparations, and lost its rights and insulted the country. Wasn't it like Japan's treatment of China today? At that time, people from all walks of life in France ran around shouting, and were sad and indignant. However, General Joffre believed that the impulse of emotion and the venting of passion could not last long, and that it was not enough to talk about saving the country without working hard at school. So he decided to study hard and specialize in military knowledge and combat skills. When the European War came, he was indeed able to save France with a bang. During the European War, Germany was beaten to pieces by the countries of the world, and was almost unrecognizable. However, Germany did not perish in the end, and is now turning from weak to strong. Why is this? This is entirely due to the existence of its national soul 丨 academic 丨. Ibsen also told us, [If you want to dedicate yourself to society, it is not enough to succeed unless you cast yourself, this piece of material, into a sharp weapon.] What a far-sighted view this is! Without real and sufficient knowledge and talent, how can you lead the people to save the country and resist foreign insults? Dear young people, these are all good examples that tell us how to save the country fundamentally. Therefore, brothers feel that the path that our national salvation movement should take now, and the fundamental method, is to sit in the library and the laboratory earnestly and carefully to study, invent, manufacture, reform, and enrich the life force of our nation, the lifeline of the country, and the spirit of society. This kind of intellectual preparation of ours is the preparation of national strength. If the national strength is sound, are we still afraid that the national shame will not be avenged? However, young people, books can be read, but dead books cannot be read. During this period of national crisis, we must also step up military training, make physical preparations, and cultivate talents for maintaining public security in the rear. At the same time, we must also sincerely urge the government and earnestly publicize to the people, telling the people the truth about the rampant tyranny of Japan and the crisis of our current lives, and the extremely effective method of resurrection. Doing it so earnestly can wash away the shame of our nation and erase the stain on China. (B)

Shenbao Local Supplement

Tuesday, January 12, 1932, Republic of China (No Additional Fee)

Short Forum

Shanghai is a Den of Iniquity Fortunately

The Japanese newspaper carried a piece of local news, which should have been interviewed from the concession authorities, counting in the past year, just in the Public Concession area, there were 33 major murder cases, no less than 25 kidnapping cases reported to the police, and small theft cases, even more difficult to count. In total, the property stolen throughout the year was worth as much as 2,225,000 yuan. The police detained over 17,000 Chinese and foreign criminals throughout the year, and investigated a total of 18,000 cases. If calculated with the whole city, the number would be even greater. This is the explanation of [Shanghai is a den of iniquity]. Indeed, Shanghai is a den of iniquity, not only Shanghai, all cities are dens of devils, all are factories for manufacturing sins. However, if we only cite the above-mentioned murder cases, kidnapping cases, small theft cases, 2,225,000 yuan worth of stolen goods, the 17,000 Chinese and foreign criminals detained by the Public Concession police, the 18,000 cases investigated, and the number which is no less than this when counted with the whole city etc. to explain Shanghai is a den of iniquity, it is very obvious that this explanation is [unfair].

The above-mentioned crimes, such as theft, such as kidnapping, such as murder, of course, are mostly done by friends from the lower classes of society, but here we want to further ask, what about the general officials? [Only officials are allowed to set fires, and common people are not allowed to light lamps], these two common sayings have ruthlessly exposed the black curtain of politics, which of those who are respected and pampered, and who are so upright and commanding the people, is not day and day extracting the blood and sweat of the common people by knocking on the bones and sucking the marrow? Which of them is not directly or indirectly committing acts of plotting wealth and killing lives, but only the means are a little more clever, but only killing people without seeing blood, if someone can add up the stolen goods of this robbery, the number would have to be hundreds or thousands of times more than [2,225,000 yuan], the devil travels in the day, the ghost goes out at night, who can say that the devil is more skilled than the ghost? It is just that people have become accustomed to the devil raging in broad daylight, and habitually think it is [legal], is the sin of Shanghai only done by these clumsy fools with low skills, the lower-class social masses who are eating lawsuits in the police station?

Further said… Why do thefts and robberies happen? Naturally it is due to [hunger and cold pressing], why do people suffer from hunger and cold? [Behind the vermilion gates, wine and meat rot, on the roads, there are frozen bones], [a rich man's feast of wine, a poor man's half-year's rations], corrupt officials have taken away the poor man's food and clothing, but they still say, why were you hungry and cold! At the extreme of hunger and cold, the poor have to steal a little, snatch a little, it is to extend the last gasp of once or twice, but they shout loudly... You restless thugs, you heinous bandits! I want to ask…

[What right does anyone have to say... I am right, you are wrong].

Shanghai is a den of iniquity, how is it only Shanghai? At present, the thing of plotting wealth and killing lives is being planned or practiced anytime and anywhere, criminals, are everywhere, stolen goods, are everywhere, Shanghai is just a corner of the world of sin.

Canine Mass Literature

An [Ah San] Silk

An [Ah San] stood at the crossroads. He had his head wrapped in cloth, was wearing a copper-buttoned uniform, and was holding a [mourning stick] in his hand, directing the traffic. Like other [Ah Sans]. He was a [bearded man]. Under his dark purple skin, he also had the blood vessels of ordinary humans, in which surged the loyalty, diligence, and even law-abidingness and public service of his profession, no different from other [Ah Sans]. He was almost a robot, his actions and even thoughts were mechanical. In his eyes, the people, things, and events he saw were more than anyone who was not a [patrolman], but what did he feel!

In the vast crowd, two of his compatriots walked over there, a man and a woman. The man was wearing high-quality gentleman's clothing, and was also a tall and extraordinary figure. Except for his complexion, he was indeed the image of a [British man]. The woman, however, was still dressed in the style of her homeland, light silk or satin wrapped around her head, body, and legs, making it impossible for us to tell whether it was a hat, a coat, or a skirt. However, she was very young and exquisite, with the usual willow eyebrows and almond eyes, a slender neck and a long waist, so that when we looked at her skin, we would call her a [black rose]. He and she walked hand in hand, gradually approaching the standing [Ah San]. He, [Ah San], suddenly froze, just like a machine that suddenly suffered an accident. The hand he raised holding the stick suddenly stopped moving up and down, his shoulders shrugged up, his chest stuck out, and he used all his energy on his two eyes, slowly turning his neck, watching the two compatriots approach his side 丨 walk past his front 丨. But in a moment, what he saw became two shadows from the back; one like a fat cow, a giant elephant, and the other like a dependent little bird, a fluttering butterfly. After another moment, the shadow from the back turned the corner and disappeared, and only then did he seem to have relieved himself of a major responsibility, exhaling a long, deep breath, while at the same time his chest collapsed, his shoulders lowered, his head lowered, his eyes looking at the ground, as if searching for something, so that he forgot to put down the stick in his hand, and could not hear the cars waiting behind him, honking incessantly.

Popular Science

Invention of Vital Substances

Advertisements in shops, whether Eastern or Western, all like to call themselves Vitamin. The translated meaning of Vitamin is Vital Substance. The ones that have been experimentally verified and are available for application are now divided into four types: A, B, C, and D!

The amount of vital substances in food varies. For example, milk is rich in Vitamin A, eggs are rich in both Vitamins A and D, and rice bran contains Vitamin B. Spinach in Western food contains Vitamins A, B, and C. Fresh fruits, potatoes, and radishes are rich in Vitamin C. Tomatoes are rich in Vitamins B and C. Milk and flour that have been irradiated with ultraviolet light are rich in Vitamin D. In addition, newly manufactured Western medicines also contain certain vital substances. However, by means of biochemical experiments, through artificial invention, to extract pure crystalline vital substances, or to set up a method for mass production, has not yet been heard of.

Recently, Professor Enler Cbelpin, a Swedish biochemical expert, has been experimenting with manufacturing new substances that are very rich in Vitamin A. Master Ottar Rygh, a university lecturer in Norway, has been developing Vitamin C. Mr. Adolf Windauss of Germany and Messrs. E.H. Reerib U隅 and A. Van Wijk of Philips Electric Factory in the Netherlands have extracted ergot bacteria parasitic between naked rye flowers, extracted ergot oil Ergesterine, and irradiated it with ultraviolet light to produce pure crystalline Vitamin D. However, the pure crystalline form of Vitamin B has not yet been announced by any inventor.

According to the 11th century and after, before the 15th century, Green Island in northeastern America had become a new state specially built by Norwegian expatriates. At that time, the grain and vegetables of Green Island all depended on the Norwegian king to send special ships to supply them continuously. After the 15th century, the contact between Norway and Green Island suddenly ceased. The Norwegians living on the island relied on fish and meat to fill their stomachs. Before several generations, they all died. This is enough to know that meat eaters often suffer from bleeding disorders due to the lack of Vitamin C, which leads to self-destruction of their lives.

As for the lack of Vitamin A leading to physical underdevelopment, and the lack of Vitamin D leading to the occurrence of rickets, it is only limited to a part of children, not as harmful as the lack of Vitamin C. Those who lack Vitamin B are prone to beriberi, which is only encountered in tropical India. And if the rice is not degermed too much, this substance is still easy to retain, and is still far less helpless than those who lack fresh fruits and vegetables and cannot obtain Vitamin C.

★ Street Sociology ★

All Kinds of Ways of Life Xing Zi

Here, I am not writing a chronicle of life for the rich, but I want to depict a picture of [lingering death] 1) I came out of a civilian hospital in front of the Great World, and just when I got to the road, someone behind me suddenly made a strange cry. Looking back, there was a head with disheveled hair and a face as yellow and withered as wax, who stepped forward to greet me with a bitter and pleading look.

[Sir, I was originally a student at the ×× School in Japan. When the Northeast Incident happened, I returned to my country. Unfortunately, I fell ill as soon as I arrived in Shanghai. Now I don't have a penny on me, and I don't have the travel expenses to go home. Seeing that you are also a learned person, a gentleman, you should be able to pity me. No matter how much, please help me with a little travel expenses.]

I touched my body, and there was only one corner left, and I had to go to a very far place, so I simply replied to him... [I'm sorry, I don't have much money on me].

But he was not disappointed by my reply, and still followed me step by step.

[Sir, no matter how much, it's my good fortune to meet you. This is only once, there will never be a second time, and maybe I will have a day to raise my eyebrows and exhale. Who can judge a person's future based on his present?]

His words were very touching, and did not sound like the talk of a friend who specializes in [patrolling the road]. I walked to the New World, and he was still following behind me. I secretly thought... [This guy's determination and perseverance to get money is not bad].

I exchanged the only corner of double horns, left the necessary tram fare, and gave the rest to him. He diligently sent me a road, and I watched his disheveled head gradually being swallowed by the sea of people, and I felt very uneasy in my heart. Half a month later, on another road, a strange cry came from behind me again. Looking back, it was still the disheveled head and the yellow wax face, but when he saw me clearly, a disappointed sorrow suddenly emerged in his pleading eyes. He casually took out a few copper coins and gave them to him, and I said with a smile... [Friend, the three lives stone has destined us to have two meetings].

East, South, West, North

The Aviation King, Eckener

Count Zeppelin, when he initially planned to build the airship, the majority of the funding was willingly raised by enthusiastic citizens. However, as soon as it took flight, the engine broke down, and it had to land for repairs.

After the first failure, a reporter vehemently criticized him in the newspaper. Zeppelin, reading this article signed [Eckener], felt truly terrified.

After the second failure, Zeppelin, feeling disheartened and terrified, picked up the newspaper to read it again. However, this time, it surprised him greatly.

[The Zeppelin airship is another great failure, but its failure unfolds great hopes for the future. I hope Count Zeppelin can hold onto the spirit of perseverance and make a comeback.]

These sentences, filled with goodwill and sympathy, revived his sorrowful mood. From then on, Zeppelin became connected with Dr. Eckener. Yesterday's enemy became today's comrade. Therefore, Eckener inherited Zeppelin's ambition and completed the great aviation enterprise of circumnavigating the world.

Shanghai Stories

Shanghai Stories (6) Zhou Rong

× The First British Consul in Shanghai

In the twenty-third year of the Daoguang reign (i.e., November 8, 1843, Gregorian calendar), British Consul to Shanghai, Colonel Balfour (i.e., Captain George Balfour), arrived in Shanghai from Guangzhou. He had been an officer in the Indian artillery and was recommended by Pottinger to be reassigned as the Consul in Shanghai. The next day, he paid a visit to Gong Mu-jiu, the Daotai of Songjiang, Suzhou, and Taicang. Gong Mu-jiu also returned the visit on the Medusa steamship.

The first problem the British Consul faced upon arriving in Shanghai was renting a consulate. A large house with a total of fifty-two rooms was rented between the West Gate and the East Gate, with an annual rent of four hundred yuan.

When the Treaty of Nanjing was signed, Pottinger did not mention the establishment of foreign settlements. At this time, Consul Balfour and the Daotai of Songjiang, Suzhou, and Taicang discussed this issue. Initially, the Daotai did not recognize the right of foreigners to purchase land in Shanghai but allowed them to continue leasing land permanently, with lessees paying annual rent.

At that time, the land price in Shanghai was 15,000 to 35,000 copper coins per mu, with approximately one silver dollar equivalent to 1,000 copper coins. Later, due to foreigners purchasing land, the price rose to 50,000 to 60,000 copper coins per mu. However, the land rent was only 1,500 copper coins per mu per year, equivalent to about one tael of government silver.

× The Initial Scope of the Settlement

The initial establishment of the settlement did not have a fixed scope: generally, it extended east to the Huangpu River, south to the Yangjingbang Creek, north to Beijing Road, and the western boundary was yet to be determined. Later, the western boundary was expanded to Henan Road, and the included area was initially only 150 acres (each acre being equivalent to approximately 6.58 Chinese mu). The terrain within the settlement was high, originally a cultivated area with crisscrossing ditches and tombs.

When local landowners sold land to foreigners, they requested that foreigners protect the tombs and allow them to sweep the tombs on time each year. Several years after the establishment of the settlement, the area west of the current Sichuan Road was still countryside. The Bund area was originally a small path along the riverbank used by boatmen for hauling, which was sometimes submerged by the tide during high tide.

Although the scope of the settlement was defined, there was still a significant difficulty that foreigners could not overcome, which was that many landowners were unwilling to sell their land. Even if they were willing, they demanded exorbitant prices. Even after the sale, they often delayed their departure from their original homes with various excuses. Therefore, due to relocation, local residents and landowners were subjected to considerable pressure from foreigners. (To be continued)
